<p>					<description><![CDATA[

<p>The Top 10: Things To Do In the Sunshine Valley     Sunshine Valley is a picturesque destination located in British Columbia, Canada, known for its natural beauty and outdoor recreational opportunities. There are near endless things to do in the Sunshine Valley and surrounding region, here are our favourite 10!  [&#8230;]</p>




<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.liftylife.ca/things-to-do-in-sunshine-valley/">Things To Do In Sunshine Valley</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.liftylife.ca">Lifty Life</a>.</p>


]]></description><br />

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-1">

<h1 class="" style="text-align: center; --fontsize: 46; line-height: 1.1;" data-fontsize="46" data-lineheight="50.6px"><strong>The Top 10:</strong></h1>




<h1 class="" style="text-align: center; --fontsize: 46; line-height: 1.1;" data-fontsize="46" data-lineheight="50.6px"><strong style="color: var(--awb-text-color); font-family: var(--awb-text-font-family); font-size: var(--awb-font-size); font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform); background-color: var(--awb-bg-color);">Things To Do </strong><strong style="font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--h1_typography-text-transform); background-color: var(--awb-bg-color); color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size);">In the Sunshine Valley</strong></h1>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-2 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-1 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-2">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Sunshine Valley is a picturesque destination located in British Columbia, Canada, known <span style="color: #000000;">for its natural beauty and outdoor recreational opportunities. </span><span style="background-color: var(--awb-bg-color); text-align: var(--awb-content-alignment); font-family: var(--awb-text-font-family); font-size: var(--awb-font-size); font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); font-weight: var(--awb-text-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform); color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);"><span style="font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); font-weight: var(--awb-text-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform); color: #000000;">There are near endless things to do in the Sunshine Valley and </span></span><span style="background-color: var(--awb-bg-color); text-align: var(--awb-content-alignment); font-family: var(--awb-text-font-family); font-size: var(--awb-font-size); font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); font-weight: var(--awb-text-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform);">surrounding</span><span style="background-color: var(--awb-bg-color); text-align: var(--awb-content-alignment); font-family: var(--awb-text-font-family); font-size: var(--awb-font-size); font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); font-weight: var(--awb-text-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform); color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);"><span style="font-style: var(--awb-text-font-style); font-weight: var(--awb-text-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--awb-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--awb-text-transform); color: #000000;"> region, here are our favourite 10!</span></span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-3 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-2 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-3">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>1. </strong><b>Hiking and Nature Walks</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-4">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Explore the scenic trails in Sunshine Valley and immerse yourself in nature. There are several trails to choose from, ranging from easy walks to more challenging hikes. Enjoy the fresh air, beautiful landscapes, and potential wildlife sightings.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-3 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-1 hover-type-none"></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-4 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-4 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-5">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>2. </strong><b>Fishing</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-6">

<p>The area is home to several rivers and lakes, making it a great spot for fishing enthusiasts. Grab your fishing gear and try your luck at catching trout, salmon, or other freshwater fish.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-5 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-2 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1200" height="800" alt="E.C. <div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-7">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>3. </strong><b>ATV Riding</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-8">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Discover the rugged terrain of Sunshine Valley on an all-terrain vehicle (ATV). There are designated trails and areas for <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/SVATVC/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">ATV riding</a>, allowing you to explore the backcountry and enjoy an exhilarating adventure.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-7 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-8 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-9">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>4. Mountain Biking</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-10">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Bring your mountain bike and hit the trails in Sunshine Valley. With varying difficulty levels, there are options for riders of all skill levels. Ride through forests, along scenic paths, and experience the thrill of mountain biking in a stunning setting.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-9 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-4 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1280" height="853" alt="Manning Park mountain biking" title="Manning Park mountain biking" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-21479" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/bicycle-ga9c962186_1280.jpg 1280w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>5. </strong><b>Winter Activities</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-12">

<p style="text-align: justify;">During the winter months, Sunshine Valley transforms into a winter wonderland. Engage in activities like snowshoeing, cross-country skiing, or sledding. The area offers trails and facilities for these winter activities, providing opportunities for <a href="https://www.manningpark.com/winter/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">outdoor fun in the snow</a>.</p>


</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-18">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Sunshine Valley is located in close proximity to other popular destinations. Consider taking day trips to places like <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/fraser-valley-ski-resorts-manning-park-vs-sasquatch-mountain/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Manning Park</a>, Hell’s Gate, Othello Tunnels, or the Fraser River. These attractions offer additional outdoor adventures and unique experiences.</p>

</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-20">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Keep an eye out for wildlife as you explore Sunshine Valley. The area is home to various animals, including deer, elk, birds, and occasionally bears. Remember to observe wildlife from a safe distance and respect their natural habitat.</p>

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-21">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>10. </strong><b>Stargazing</b></h2>


</div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-22">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Take some time to relax and appreciate the tranquility of Sunshine Valley. The area has minimal light pollution, making it an ideal spot for stargazing. On clear nights, marvel at the vastness of the night sky and enjoy the beauty of the stars.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<div style="text-align: center;"><b style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Property Checklist for Homeowners</b></div>




<p><span style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--h1_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Supplies, Amenities, and Furnishing</span></h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-14 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-23 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-23">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Renting out your vacation home can be a great way to generate extra income while you’re not using it, but managing a rental property requires careful attention to detail. Before handing over the keys to your vacation rental, it’s important to ensure that the property is fully equipped with all the necessary amenities, supplies, and furnishings to ensure a comfortable and enjoyable stay for your guests. In this article, we will provide a comprehensive list of recommended amenities, supplies, and furnishings that homeowners should consider providing to their vacation rental guests to help ensure a positive guest experience and maximum rental income. From basic essentials like linens and towels, to more luxurious amenities like hot tubs and high-end appliances, we’ll cover everything you need to know to make your vacation rental stand out from the competition.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-15 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-24 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-24">

<h3 class="" style="text-align: left; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Checklists</b></h3>

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>1. Kitchen Checklist</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">This checklist covers all items that should be supplied within your kitchen. This includes all the obvious supplies and amenities but also extends to items that you may not immediately think of until a guest asks “where is the can opener?” It can be easy to forget a few crucial amenities; use our guide to help minimize these oversights.</p>

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>3. Laundry Room Checklist</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">We highly recommend purchasing spares sets of linens and towels to ensure we always have a backup set in case a linen becomes soiled. The best rule of thumb is to have three sets per bed, a clean set, dirty set, and spare set. In addition to overstocking make sure to protect your mattresses and pillows with covers and pads.</p>

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-37">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>4. Property Furnishing Checklist</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Furnishing your home is where you get to be creative and put in your own style. Airbnb’s are meant to be unique spaces so don’t be afraid to put your own quirky flair on your property. Make an effort to <a href="https://www.pinterest.ca/lifty_life" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">create spaces that truly stand out</a>. Travelling guests are looking for something different and provides a locals experience.</p>

<li><a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07D388KVH/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#038;camp=1789&#038;creative=9325&#038;creativeASIN=B07D388KVH&#038;linkCode=as2&#038;tag=liftylife0c-20&#038;linkId=37d458cbb3a4c4b238c054f8e9efa224" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Noise Monitoring</a></li>




<li><a href="https://amzn.to/3KYhpFU" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Ring Doorbell</a></li>




<li><a href="https://amzn.to/3LlOjl2" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Motion Sensor Lighting</a></li>




<li><a href="https://amzn.to/3LlJAQo" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Locked Closet</a></li>


</ul>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-67 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:70px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

										<content:encoded><![CDATA[

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-40 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-68 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-49">

<h1 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 46; line-height: 1.1;" data-fontsize="46" data-lineheight="50.6px"><b>How To Setup An Airbnb</b></h1>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-41 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-69 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-50">

<p>Welcome to the world of Airbnb hosting! If you’re new to the game and feeling a bit overwhelmed, don’t worry – you’re not alone. Setting up an Airbnb can be a lot of work, but with the right planning and preparation, it can also be a lot of fun. In this article, we’re going to walk you through the process step by step and give you some helpful tips and tricks to make your journey as smooth and successful as possible. So grab a cup of coffee, put your feet up, and let’s get started on creating the perfect Airbnb!</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-42 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-70 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-testimonials classic fusion-testimonials-1" style="--awb-textcolor:#747474;--awb-backgroundcolor:#f6f6f6;" data-random="0" data-speed="4000">

<div class="reviews">

<div class="review active-testimonial avatar-image">

<blockquote><q class="fusion-clearfix">


<p><em>“At Lifty Life, we understand the importance of streamlining operations for Airbnb hosts. That’s why we highly recommend utilizing home automation technologies to automate tasks and improve efficiency. One quick tip for new hosts is to invest in a smart lock for easy self-check-in and check-out for guests, as well as a smart thermostat to easily control the temperature in the space remotely.”</em></p>


</q></blockquote>



<div class="author"><span class="testimonial-thumbnail"><img decoding="async" class="testimonial-image" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/circle-cropped.png" width="569" height="569" alt="connor griffiths" /></span><span class="company-name"><strong>Connor Griffiths</strong>, <span>CEO of Lifty Life</span></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-43 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-71 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;width:100%;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-44 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-72 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-51">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>Staging and Interior Design for your Airbnb</strong></h2>




<p><strong>Start by decluttering your space. </strong>Get rid of anything that you don’t need or use, and make sure the space is clean and organized. Start by going room by room and taking everything out of closets, drawers, and cabinets. Sort through your items and decide what to keep, what to donate, and what to throw away. Once your space is decluttered, give it a deep clean. This will make it feel fresh and new and will give you a clean slate to work with.</p>




<ul>


<li>Look for second-hand furniture and decor at thrift stores, garage sales, or online marketplaces.</li>




<li>Look for pieces that can be repurposed or refreshed with a coat of paint or new hardware.</li>




<li>Consider rearranging the furniture or using it in a different room than intended to give it a new look.</li>


</ul>




<p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-21229" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully.png" alt="photo of fern gull which is clutter free" width="1200" height="628" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-200x105-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-300x157-1.png 300w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-400x209-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-600x314-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-768x402-1.png 768w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-800x419-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully-1024x536-1.png 1024w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-Fern-Gully.png 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" /></p>




<p><strong>Use neutral colors for the walls and furniture.</strong> This will help make the space feel more inviting and will be more appealing to potential guests. Neutral colors include shades of white, gray, beige, and taupe. These colors are calming and soothing and will help create a sense of spaciousness in the room. You can add pops of color with accessories such as throw pillows, blankets, or artwork.</p>




<ul>


<li>Look for paint samples at your local home improvement store or online.</li>




<li>Choose a neutral color that will be more appealing to potential guests.</li>




<li>Consider painting just one wall as an accent wall to bring some color to the space without overwhelming it.</li>




<li>Read our article on <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/how-to-decorate-your-airbnb-vacation-rental/">how to decorate your Airbnb</a></li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Use high-quality linens and towels.</strong> This will make the space feel more luxurious and will help guests feel more comfortable. Invest in high-quality bedding, such as 100% cotton sheets, and fluffy white towels. Make sure to have extra sets of linens on hand for guests, and consider providing a robe and slippers for added comfort.</p>




<ul>


<li>Look for deals on textiles at discount stores or online marketplaces.</li>




<li>Use throw pillows, blankets and curtains to add warmth and texture to the space.</li>




<li>Use different patterns and textures to create interest and depth in the space.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Add some personal touches, like plants or artwork.</strong> This will help make the space feel more like a home and will be more inviting to guests. Plants can help purify the air, and art can add personality to the space. You can add a few small plants to the room, like succulents or herbs, and choose artwork that reflects the style of your space.</p>




<ul>


<li>Look for plants in your local community, or ask friends or family if they have any to give away.</li>




<li>You can also take cuttings from plants you already have and propagate them.</li>




<li>Place the plants in different areas of the room to create a cohesive and natural look.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Take high-quality photos of your space. </strong>These photos will be the first thing that potential guests see, so it’s important to make a good first impression. Use a good camera and take photos during the day when there is plenty of natural light. Take photos of each room, including the kitchen and bathroom, and make sure to capture any special Use natural light: Natural light can be used to create stunning and dramatic photographs. Take advantage of the natural light available in the room, such as sunlight streaming through windows or skylights.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Use a tripod:</strong> Using a tripod will help you keep your camera steady and eliminate any camera shake, which can blur your photos. A tripod also allows you to shoot at slower shutter speeds without the need for a flash.</li>




<li><strong>Use a wide-angle lens:</strong> A wide-angle lens will allow you to capture more of the room in a single photograph and can also create an illusion of space.</li>




<li><strong>Use editing software:</strong> Post-processing your photos can help you correct color, adjust brightness and contrast, and remove any unwanted elements from the photograph. Some popular editing software options include Lightroom and Photoshop.</li>




<li><strong>Experiment with different angles and perspectives:</strong> Try shooting from different angles and perspectives to create more interesting and dynamic photos. Take photos from above, below, and at eye level to give a good sense of the space.</li>




<li><strong>Hire a professional photographer:</strong> If you don’t feel confident in your photography skills, you can hire a professional photographer to take high-quality photos of your property. Look for a photographer who specializes in real estate photography and has a portfolio of work that you like.</li>


</ul>




<p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-21228" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook.png" alt="photo of the overlook which uses a wide angle lense" width="1200" height="628" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-200x105-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-300x157-1.png 300w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-400x209-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-600x314-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-768x402-1.png 768w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-800x419-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook-1024x536-1.png 1024w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-the-overlook.png 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" /></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-45 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-73 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-52">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><strong>Home Automation for your Airbnb</strong></h2>




<p>Home automation can be a great way for Airbnb hosts to improve operational efficiency and enhance the guest experience. Setting up your home with some of the state-of-the-art <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/airbnb-smart-home-and-devices/">smart home devices</a> can really help elevate the percieved value of your property. Here are some tips on how to set up home automation in your Airbnb:</p>




<p><strong>Invest in a smart lock.</strong> Smart locks allow guests to check in and out of your property without the need for keys. This can save you time and hassle, and it also provides an added layer of security for your property. Some popular smart lock options include August Smart Lock and Nest x Yale Lock. To install a smart lock, you will need to first purchase the lock and then follow the manufacturer’s instructions for installation.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>August Smart Lock Pro:</strong> This lock allows guests to enter the property using their smartphone, and it also includes a keypad for guests who prefer to use a code. It also has a feature called “Auto-Unlock” that automatically unlocks the door when the guest is near the property.</li>




<li><strong>Schlage Sense Smart Deadbolt</strong>: This lock allows guests to enter the property using their smartphone and also includes a keypad. It also has a feature that allows you to set up to 30 access codes for guests, cleaners, or other people who may need access to the property.</li>




<li><strong>Kwikset 916 Smart Lock:</strong> This lock allows guests to enter the property using their smartphone, and it also includes a keypad. It has a feature called “SmartKey Security” that helps to prevent lock picking and bumping.</li>




<li><strong>Nest x Yale Lock:</strong> This lock allows guests to enter the property using their smartphone, and it also includes a keypad. It has a feature called “Auto-Lock” that automatically locks the door after it’s been opened and left unlocked for a certain period of time.</li>




<li><b>Keycafe:</b> In some situations a smart lock might not work for the checkin process. As an alternative consider using a smart key management system such as <a href="https://www.keycafe.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Keycafe</a>.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Set up a smart thermostat.</strong> Smart thermostats allow you to control the temperature in your property remotely, which can save you money on energy costs. Additionally, it provides guests with the ability to control the temperature in the space, which can improve their experience. Some <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/best-airbnb-smart-locks/">popular smart thermostat options</a> include Nest Learning Thermostat and Ecobee Smart Thermostat.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Nest Learning Thermostat:</strong> This thermostat learns your temperature preferences over time and can automatically adjust the temperature based on your schedule. It also has a feature called “Remote Control” that allows you to adjust the temperature from your smartphone.</li>




<li><strong>Ecobee SmartThermostat: </strong>This thermostat has a feature called “Room Sensors” that can detect temperature and occupancy in different rooms, allowing you to adjust the temperature accordingly.</li>




<li><strong>Honeywell T9 Smart Thermostat:</strong> This thermostat has a feature called “Geofencing” that can detect when you’re away from home and automatically adjust the temperature accordingly.</li>




<li><strong>Sensi Touch Smart Thermostat:</strong> This thermostat allows you to control the temperature from your smartphone, and it also has a feature called “Vacation Mode” that allows you to set a specific temperature schedule when you’re away from home.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Use smart lighting.</strong> Smart lighting allows you to control the lighting in your property remotely, which can save you money on energy costs. Additionally, it provides guests with the ability to control the lighting in the space, which can improve their experience. Some popular smart lighting options include Philips Hue and LIFX.</p>




<p><strong>Install a smart security camera.</strong> A smart security camera can provide an added layer of security for your property and can also help you keep an eye on your property while you’re away. Some popular smart security camera options include Nest Cam and Ring Spotlight Cam. Always remember that no cameras should be inside the unit. All cameras need to be exterior cameras and need to be disclosed to your guests.</p>




<p><strong>Use a smart home hub.</strong> A smart home hub can be used to control all of your smart devices in one place. This can make it easier for you to manage your devices and can also improve the guest experience by allowing them to control all of the smart devices in the property from one central location. Some popular smart home hub options include Amazon Echo and Google Home.</p>




<p>By implementing these home automation tips, you can save time and money while providing guests with a more comfortable and convenient experience.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-46 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-74 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-53">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><strong>Using Vacation Rental Software to Setup &#038; Automate Your Airbnb</strong></h2>




<p><strong>Use a property management system (PMS) to streamline your operations.</strong> A PMS can help you keep track of reservations, communicate with guests, and handle payments and billing. Some <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/airbnb-vacation-rental-software/">popular PMS options</a> include Lodgify, Guesty, and Hostaway. A good PMS should allow you to manage all aspects of your property in one place, from listing management, to reservations, to guest communication, and financial reports.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Guesty:</strong> This system offers a wide range of features, including reservation management, guest communication, and task automation. It also has a feature called “Integrated Channel Management” that allows you to manage multiple platforms from one central location.</li>




<li><strong>Hostaway:</strong> This system allows you to manage reservations, guest communications, and financial reports all in one place. It also offers automated pricing and inventory management, as well as integrations with popular payment gateways. Read our in-depth <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/vacation-rental-software-review-hostaway/">review of Hostaway</a> and why we recommend it to everyone.</li>




<li><strong>Lodgify:</strong> This system allows you to manage reservations, guest communications, and financial reports all in one place. It also has a feature called “Website Builder” that allows you to create a professional website for your property.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Implement dynamic pricing software to optimize your pricing strategy.</strong> Dynamic pricing software can help you automatically adjust your prices based on demand and other factors, allowing you to maximize your revenue and fill more of your calendar. Some popular dynamic pricing software options include Beyond Pricing, PriceLabs, and Smartbnb.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Beyond Pricing:</strong> This software uses machine learning to adjust your prices based on demand and competition. It also includes features such as real-time price tracking, market intelligence and setting of custom pricing rules.</li>




<li><strong>PriceLabs:</strong> This software allows you to set custom pricing rules based on factors such as occupancy, seasonality and time of booking. It also includes features such as real-time price tracking, revenue forecasting and it supports multiple channels.</li>




<li><strong>Wheelhouse:</strong> This software allows you to set custom pricing rules based on factors such as occupancy, seasonality and time of booking. It also includes features such as real-time price tracking, revenue forecasting, and it integrates with property management systems.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Utilize channel management software to reach more potential guests.</strong> Channel management software can help you list and manage your property on multiple vacation rental platforms, such as Airbnb, Booking.com, and VRBO, from one central location. This can save you a lot of time and help you reach more potential guests. Some popular channel management software options include Wheelhouse, Staah, and Rentals United.</p>




<p><strong>Use cleaning and maintenance software to ensure your property is always in top condition.</strong> This type of software can help you keep track of cleaning schedules, maintenance tasks, and inventory, and can also help you communicate with cleaning and maintenance staff. This can help you ensure that your property is always in top condition for guests. Some popular cleaning and maintenance software options include Guesty, Hostaway, and Hosty.</p>




<p>By using vacation rental software regularly, you can improve your operations, increase your revenue, and provide a better experience for your guests. Remember to do your research and choose the software that best fits your needs and budget. Also, keep in mind that most of these software offers free trial periods, it’s always a good idea to test them before committing.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-47 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-75 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-54">

<h2><strong>How You Setup Your Airbnb Will Dictate How Your Market It</strong></h2>




<p><strong>Branding:</strong> Create a unique and memorable brand for your property, this can include a catchy name, a logo, and a consistent design aesthetic. By branding your property, it will have a higher perceived value and help it stand out in the crowded vacation rental market.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Choose a color palette:</strong> Pick a color palette that reflects the overall style and theme of your property. Use this color palette throughout the property, in everything from paint and linens to artwork and accessories.</li>




<li><strong>Use a consistent design aesthetic:</strong> Choose a design aesthetic that reflects the overall style and theme of your property. Use this aesthetic throughout the property, in everything from furniture and decor to artwork and accessories.</li>




<li><strong>Create a unique name:</strong> Give your property a unique name that reflects the overall style and theme of the property. This will help it stand out in the crowded vacation rental market.</li>




<li><strong>Create a logo:</strong> Create a logo that reflects the overall style and theme of the property. Use this logo throughout your listing, website, and social media accounts.</li>




<li><strong>Add personal touches:</strong> Add personal touches to the property that reflect the overall style and theme of the property. This can be done by adding artwork, plants, or any other items that will make the space feel welcoming and homey.</li>


</ul>




<p><strong>Thoughtful touches:</strong> Include thoughtful touches like a bottle of wine, gourmet coffee beans, eco-friendly soaps and shampoos, and other amenities that will make your guests feel special and appreciated. This can help create a memorable experience for your guests and encourage them to return.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Welcome gifts:</strong> Provide a welcome gift for guests such as a bottle of wine, a basket of locally-sourced treats, or a small plant.</li>




<li><strong>Personalized notes:</strong> Leave personalized notes for guests in the property to make them feel welcome and appreciated.</li>




<li><strong>Local guidebooks:</strong> Provide guests with a guidebook of local recommendations for things to do, see, and eat.</li>




<li><strong>Fresh flowers:</strong> Add fresh flowers to the property to create a welcoming and inviting atmosphere.</li>




<li><strong>Personalized decor:</strong> Add personalized decor to the property that reflects the local area, such as artworks, photographs, or other decorative items.</li>


</ul>




<p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-21227" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake.png" alt="photo of harrison on the lake which has lots of unique touches" width="1200" height="628" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-200x105-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-300x157-1.png 300w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-400x209-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-600x314-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-768x402-1.png 768w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-800x419-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake-1024x536-1.png 1024w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/photo-of-harrison-on-the-lake.png 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" /></p>




<p><strong>Detailed listing:</strong> Create a detailed listing that includes all of the most important amenities that Airbnb offers, such as a full kitchen, wifi, and air conditioning. Ensuring you have a lot of amenities is one of the key factors to<a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/how-to-rank-on-airbnb/"> ranking high on Airbnb’s search algorithm</a>. Be sure to also include information about the location, nearby attractions, and any special features of the property.</p>




<ul>


<li><strong>Wi-Fi:</strong> A reliable and fast internet connection is a must-have for most guests.</li>




<li><strong>Television:</strong> A TV with cable or streaming services access is a common amenity.</li>




<li><strong>Kitchen:</strong> A fully equipped kitchen with appliances, cookware, and utensils is a common amenity.</li>




<li><strong>Bed linens and towels:</strong> Clean and comfortable bed linens and towels are a must-have for guests.</li>




<li><strong>Air conditioning or heating</strong>: Climate control is an important amenity that guests expect.</li>




<li><strong>Washer and dryer:</strong> A laundry facility is a common amenity in long-term rentals.</li>




<li><strong>Parking:</strong> Off-street or on-site parking is a common amenity.</li>




<li><strong>Iron and ironing board:</strong> These are amenities that guests often need, but don’t always think to ask for.</li>




<li><strong>Hair dryer:</strong> A hair dryer is a common amenity that guests expect.</li>




<li><strong>Basic toiletries:</strong> Basic toiletries such as soap, shampoo, and toilet paper are essential amenities that guests expect.</li>




<li><strong>Smoke and Carbon Monoxide detectors:</strong> these are important for guest’s safety and a requirement by most local laws.</li>


</ul>




<p>There are so many amenities and items that are needed for your property, that is why we created a thorough <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/str-amenities-checklist/">amenities checklist</a> that helps you ensure you don’t miss anything!</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-48 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-76 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-55">

<h2><strong>Conclusion</strong></h2>




<p>Setting up an Airbnb property can be a great way to make extra income, but it also requires careful planning and preparation. It is important to pay attention to the details when it comes to staging and interior design, using smart home technology to improve operational efficiency and guest experience and using property management software to streamline your operations. Additionally, using dynamic pricing software to optimize your prices in real-time can help you stay competitive in the market. By following these tips and tricks, you can set up an Airbnb property that is both profitable and enjoyable for guests to stay in. Remember to always be prepared to adapt to the market and guest’s needs, and to always strive to improve your property, and you will be on the path to success.</p>




<h3><strong>Lifty Life Can Help Take The Stress Out Of The Day-to-Day Worries Of Operating and Airbnb</strong></h3>




<p>Do you enjoy setting up your Airbnb, but don’t actually want to be faced with the daily operational issuing of managing your own Airbnb property? Let Lifty Life take the reins and turn your property into a relatively passive income stream. With our comprehensive <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/services/">Airbnb management services</a>, you can sit back and relax while we handle everything from guest communications to maintenance and cleaning. We’ll even include unlimited homeowner usage, so you can still enjoy your property when it’s not being rented out. Plus, with our advanced pricing strategies, you can trust that you’re getting the most out of your rental. Don’t wait any longer, contact us today!</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<h1 style="text-align: center;"><strong>Guide To: Buying a Vacation Rental</strong></h1>

</h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-50 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-78 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-56">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Are you interested in the short term rental real (STR) estate market? There is a lot to learn so you’ve come to the right place. Vacation rentals are very different to residential real estate in the goals, analysis, opportunity, and financing. This article details everything you should know when starting on your path to buy a short term rental.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">As a management company for vacation rentals and as investors ourselves we’ve gone through this before and helped many buyers in selecting, analyzing, and managing their units. This article is a summary of all the lessons we’ve learned over the years.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-51 fusion-flex-container has-pattern-background has-mask-background nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;--awb-margin-bottom:30px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-79 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-testimonials classic fusion-testimonials-2" style="--awb-textcolor:#747474;--awb-backgroundcolor:#f6f6f6;" data-random="0" data-speed="4000">

<div class="reviews">

<div class="review active-testimonial avatar-image">

<blockquote><q class="fusion-clearfix">


<blockquote>


<p>“Owning a vacation rental property is not just an investment in real estate, it’s an investment in memories, experiences, and the opportunity to create a home away from home for your guests. The benefits of investing in a vacation rental property go far beyond financial gains, as it allows you to provide a unique and personalized experience for travelers while also creating a source of passive income for yourself.”</p>


</blockquote>


</q></blockquote>



<div class="author"><span class="testimonial-thumbnail"><img decoding="async" class="testimonial-image" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Bio-Picture-March-20-2019.jpeg" width="1019" height="1009" alt="Keiran Griffiths bio shot" style="--awb-border-radius:50px;" /></span><span class="company-name"><strong>Keiran Griffiths</strong>, <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/keirangriffiths/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>CMO of Lifty Life + Real Estate Investor</span></a></span></div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-52 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-80 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-53 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-81 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-57">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>Where Should I Buy a Vacation Rental?</strong></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Deciding where to buy a vacation rental starts with understanding your goals, identifying attractive markets, and then weighing opportunity and risk. Short-term rentals have been successful in urban, suburban, remote, and rural markets however not all markets are made equal or will fit your needs. In our experience vacation markets and major downtown metro markets are the best performers. These are the markets that Lifty Life chooses to focus our buying and managing in.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-54 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-82 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-58">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Understanding your Goals</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">It’s easy to get excited about the idea of buying a vacation home. Who wouldn’t want a ski-in ski-out home on Whistler or an oceanfront cabin in Tofino but at some point you need to come back to reality and understand your goals and risk tolerance.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Before selecting the market you’ll need to ask yourself why am I buying this property? <span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Here are some common reasons for buying a vacation rental or home:</span></p>




<blockquote style="text-align: justify;">


<p><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); font-weight: bold; background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);">Getaways </span><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">– you want to use the property for your family, friend, and personal getaways and rent it short-term to help cover the cost of ownership.</span></p>




<div style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);"><b>Investment</b> </span><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);">– the primary goal of buying a vacation property is as an investment.</span></div>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);"><b>Personal Use*</b> </span><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);">– this is your dream home. You may choose to never rent it or hardly ever. If you do it’s only for top dollar or to close friends and family.</span></p>




<div style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);"><b>I’m There All the Time</b> </span><span style="color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);">– you often visit {destination} for work or visiting family and are purchasing a short term rental that can house you on these trips and be rented the rest of the time.</span></div>


</blockquote>




<p><b>*</b>This article focuses on buying a vacation home that will be rented part of full time.<span style="text-align: justify; background-color: var(--testimonial_bg_color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"><br /></span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-55 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-83 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-59">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Selecting a Market</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The next question to ask yourself is “which region best fits my goals and budget?”</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">There are generally three types of markets that you can purchase a short-term rental in: metro markets, major vacation markets, and staycation markets. In many cases there is overlap on these categories, Kelowna for example falls in all three.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>
