<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-85 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-60">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Proximity to Where you Live</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The close proximity of your short-term rental to where you live is less important than you might <span style="color: #000000;">think. Sure there is a level of comfort in knowing you can be there in a couple </span><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><span style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); color: #000000;">hours but is that really necessary? Are you really the one that should be fixing a broken sink? Is it really worth your time to </span></span><span style="color: #000000;">deliver</span><span style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); color: #000000;"> the guest a roll of </span></span><span style="color: #ba0000;"><span style="color: #000000;">toilet</span></span><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"> paper? 99% of the time the answer is no.</span></span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">In the majority of markets there are people that can help with the operational side of owning a vacation home. You can hire a cleaner, handyman, or even a <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/services/full-service/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">full service management company</a> like Lifty Life (</span></span>shameless<span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"> plug) to maintain your property, run the operations, and keep guests happy. These services minimize the risk of owning a distant vacation property.</span></span></span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-58 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-86 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-61">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Supply and Demand</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Here is your economics 101 lesson: prices are highest in markets with high demand and low supply, prices are lowest in markets with low demand and high supply. The principles of supply and demand extend to both the real estate and the vacation rental world so it is something to really consider.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Take Tofino for example, the region is tiny, there are very few homes, and housing demand is huge. Unsurprisingly the real estate market there is hot and it’s even hotter for the select few buildings that are short-term rental friendly. The benefit of this region is because there is such a low supply of vacation rentals the average nightly rates are among the highest in the country.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-59 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-87 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-62">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Zoning &#038; Bylaw Regulations</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Before buying a property or setting your mind on a market you’ll need to understand the short term rental rules in that community. The restrictions on short term rentals are primarily on the municipal level in the form of zoning bylaws and business licensing. Check the municipal website in that community for clarification on the rules related to short term rentals. Don’t make the mistake of buying a home in a zoning that isn’t rental friendly.</p>

</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-89 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-63">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>What Type of Vacation Rental Should I Buy?</strong></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">This question mostly comes down to the numbers. What can you afford? How much will the property reasonably generate? What will it cost to operate and maintain the property? When considering what to buy consider the property type, number of bedrooms, amenities such as pools, hot tubs, laundry, and the kitchen.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-62 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-90 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-64">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>To Strata or Not to Strata</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Condos and townhomes are the most affordable property types and have a lot of great benefits beyond the sticker price but certainly can have some negatives. “Strata corporations” and “strata fees” are terrifying words for many investors. The idea of a group of tyrannical and incompetent Karen’s running the the strata council is the first thing that comes to mind for many. Fortunately vacation market strata’s tend to operate better than their suburban counterparts. The reason is the majority of owners are either investors or second home owners. The goals of these types of owners is to have the strata be run well, the bylaws to remain rental friendly, and the value of the real estate to be protected.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Strata fees will impact your profitability but they can offer a lot of value. Building maintenance, insurance, security, utilities, are all commonly covered expenses in your strata fees. Strata complexes can also have building amenities such as gyms, pools, hot tubs, secure parking, that can all be great for attracting travelers. However keep in mind, the more building amenities the higher your strata fees and higher the likelihood of a future levy.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-63 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-91 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-65">

<h3><b>Selecting a Niche: Luxury, Mid-Range, or Budget</b><b></b></h3>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-64 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-92 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-66">

<h4 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>Luxury Vacation Homes</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The luxury segment of vacation rentals has the highest ceiling for earnings. Amazing properties in great locations can rent for $800+ per night. High-end furnishings, high-quality amenities, and a great guest experience are needed for this segment. Unsurprisingly these are also the most expensive properties to purchase, furnish, and set-up.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-93 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:90px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-12 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="The Overlook - Harrison Hot Springs" title="The Overlook – Harrison Hot Springs" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-21115" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/C___8244-2-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-94 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-68">

<h4 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>Mid-Range Vacation Homes</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The mid-range segment of the market is the category that the majority of listings fall under. This is therefore the most crowded segment but stills remains attractive. Rates in this segment range between $150 to as much as $1,000 depending on the market. To stand out in this segment focus on providing a unique and eye-catching property and interior.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-95 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:86.9972px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-70">

<h4 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>Budget Vacation Homes</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The budget segment can actually be a very attractive market in the short term rental industry. Properties in this market typically range in price from $50 to $250 a night. Depending on the property you choose to purchase you may be best suited to compete in providing superior value to budget and staycation travelers.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-97 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:87.9972px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-72">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Amenities: Pools, Hot Tubs, and More</b></h3>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-68 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-99 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-73">

<p style="text-align: justify;">You may be wondering about the value that hot tubs, pools, and other major amenities add to the nightly rate of your property. There is no perfect calculation for this but here are some general estimates that should help. The impact of these amenities may instead impact your occupancy rate.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-100 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">


<div class="table-2">


<table width="100%">


<thead>


<tr>


<th style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>Amenity </strong></th>




<th style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>+ Nightly Rate</strong></th>


</tr>


</thead>




<tbody>


<tr>


<td style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>Pool</strong></td>




<td style="text-align: center;" align="left">$100 – $150</td>


</tr>




<tr>


<td style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>Hot Tub</strong></td>




<td style="text-align: center;" align="left">$30 – $40</td>


</tr>




<tr>


<td style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>Laundry</strong></td>




<td style="text-align: center;" align="left">$10 – $15</td>


</tr>




<tr>


<td style="text-align: center;" align="left"><strong>Pet-Friendly</strong></td>




<td style="text-align: center;" align="left"><a href="https://getpaidforyourpad.com/blog/airbnb-pet-friendly-2/">$25 – $50 / pet</a></td>


</tr>


</tbody>


</table>


</div>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-69 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-101 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-74">

<p style="text-align: justify;">When providing major amenities such as pools or hot tubs you must consider the ongoing maintenance which can be very costly. If offering a pet-friendly space also consider the extra cleaning and risk of increased ware and tare.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-70 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-102 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-75">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Buying Furnished STR Real Estate</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Often in vacation markets units are sold fully furnished. This can be a great benefit but not always. The reason that owners sell fully furnished is because the contents of the property are likely heavily rented and the cost to move the items is a hassle. For this reason contents are not valued when setting the asking price and shouldn’t be considered as part of your offer price.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Purchasing a furnished rental can lower the set-up costs and expediate the Go-Live time for getting it rented on Airbnb. However be prepared to replace items over time. When you get the keys do an audit of the entire property, replace items that need replacing, spruce up the space, and dispose of unwanted contents.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-71 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-103 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-74 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-107 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-78">

<h2><strong>How Much Will My Vacation Rental Make?</strong></h2>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-75 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-108 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-79">

<p style="text-align: justify;">How much will this property make is probably the number one question I get asked at Lifty Life. Potential owners are looking for a property that at a minimum will cover its expenses or better yet profit! The truth is it’s hard to know. Each property is unique and market conditions are ever-changing. Plus most owners have a misunderstanding of the costs associated with operating a property. That being said there are a lot of tools and experience that the team at Lifty Life uses to make forecasts.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-76 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-109 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-80">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Understanding the Seasonality of the Market</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Seasonality is a foreign word for long term rental owners but it is crucial to understand in the short term rental industry. Depending on your market you might actually lose money part of the year and need to make it all up in a short peak season. But even in four season markets you will notice that seasonality exists and will need to prepare and strategize for it.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Understanding the seasonality of your market might not be as easy as you think and many times potential buyers get it wrong. Take Canmore, Alberta for example; Canmore is the neighbouring community of Banff, Alberta and a fantastic rental market. The region has 4 ski resorts within an hour drive so potential buyers assume that the winter is an amazing season some even mistake it as the peak season.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-77 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-110 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-81">

<p style="text-align: justify;">However the reality it quite different. Summer in Banff and Canmore is undeniably peak season as shown in red on the calendar. Winter pails in comparison to the income that is earned within the Summer.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-111 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-17 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1025" height="771" alt="Canmore, Alberta Seasonality" title="Canmore, Alberta Seasonality" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21027" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257-200x150-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257-400x301-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257-600x451-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257-800x602-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-18-124257.png 1025w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-78 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-112 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-82">

<p style="text-align: justify;">Why is this important? Because a misunderstanding of seasonality means you will have a misunderstanding of your cash flow and a misunderstanding of cashflow is a recipe for disaster. Understand the seasonality to manage your cash flow throughout the year and remember cash in the bank doesn’t necessarily mean you’ve profited.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-79 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-113 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-83">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Revenue Forecasting</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">To forecast your revenue the best tool on the market is <a href="https://airdna.grsm.io/kwc0oyv7pplw" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Airdna</a>. Simply provide the address, number of beds, baths, and guests to the Rentalizer tool.</p>




<blockquote>


<p><span style="font-style: normal;">Read our <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/vacation-rental-software-review-airdna/">Airdna re<span style="color: #000000;">view here</span></a></span></p>


</blockquote>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Alternatively reach out to a local Airbnb manager to get their insights on the revenue potential of your property. Lifty Life for example provides revenue estimates for properties within our <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/destinations/">service regions</a>.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Another amazing way to get revenue projections is to ask the owner for their financials (this assumes it is an STR).</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-114 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:93px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-18 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1565" height="2383" alt="Airdna Rentalizer" title="Airdna Rentalizer" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21080" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53-200x305-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53-400x609-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53-600x914-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53-800x1218-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53-1200x1827-1.png 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/screencapture-airdna-co-vacation-rental-data-app-ca-alberta-calgary-rentalizer-2022-08-26-13_02_53.png 1565w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-80 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-115 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-84">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Expense Forecasting</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">When forecasting your costs you’ll need to estimate your set-up costs, variable expenses, recurring expenses, and annual maintenance, The best way to forecast expenses is research. To do this grab some quotes from contractors, look for costs on MLS listings, and understand the fees of OTA sites.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-81 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-116 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-85">

<h4 class="" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>1. Set-Up Costs</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Among the set-up costs for your short-term rental are your down payment, closing costs, furnishing the property, stocking the unit with consumables, and adding smart home devices such as digital locks.</p>




<blockquote>


<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"><b>1. Down Payment</b></span><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"> &#038; Closing</span></strong><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"><strong> –</strong> the down payment depends entirely on your financing strategy but 20% of purchase price is typical. We discuss financing options later in the article. You can </span></span><a href="https://wowa.ca/calculators/closing-costs"><span style="font-style: normal;">estimate</span><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"> your closing cost with this tool</span></span></a><span style="font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family);"><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">.</span></span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"><strong>2. Furnishing &#038; Stocking </strong>– these expenses can vary widely but a good frame of reference is $5000 per bedroom to furnish the full home. Use our </span><a style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);" href="https://www.liftylife.ca/str-amenities-checklist/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Short Term Rental Checklist</a><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"> to outfit your property and <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/vacation-rental-replenishment/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">our stocking list</a>.</span></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-82 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-117 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-86">

<h4><b>2. Variable Fees &#038; Expenses</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Variable expenses include the costs to clean and replenish between stays and the fees of Airbnb, VRBO, and other online travel agencies (OTAs). Depending on the sales channel you may also need to cover credit card processing. Taxes and management fees must also be considered when expense forecasting.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-83 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-118 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-87">

<blockquote>


<p class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);"><b><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal);">3. Cleaning &#038;</span> </b></span><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); font-style: normal;"><b>Replenishment – </b>the cost to clean varies by region and property type. Get quotes from local cleaning companies to estimate this expense.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>4. OTA &#038; Credit Card Fees </b><span style="font-size: 19px;" data-fusion-font="true"><b>– </b>OTAs fees include the charges made by sites like <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/airbnb-vs-vrbo/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Airbnb and VRBO</a>. Airbnb charges a 3% host fee and ~14% mark up to guests. VRBO charges a 5% host fee, 3% credit card processing, and 6-12% mark up.</span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>5. Management Fees – </b>hiring a manager or not you should forecast this cost. This allows you to value the work needed to manage the property. As a reference <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/services/prices/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Lifty Life charges a 25% commission</a>.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>6. Taxes </b>– will vary by province and municipality. GST, PST, and local tourism taxes are all applicable. Whistler for example the taxes are GST (5%), <a href="https://www2.gov.bc.ca/assets/gov/taxes/sales-taxes/publications/pst-120-accommodation.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">PST (8%)</a>, and <a href="https://members.whistler.com/mrdt/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">MDRT (3%)</a>.</span></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-119 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-19 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1080" height="1080" alt="Lifty Life Fee Breakdown" title="Lifty Life Fee Breakdown" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21108" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3-200x200-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3-400x400-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3-600x600-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3-800x800-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-3.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-120 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-20 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1080" height="1080" alt="Lifty Life Fee Breakdown 2" title="Lifty Life Fee Breakdown 2" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21109" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4-200x200-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4-400x400-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4-600x600-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4-800x800-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Fee-Chart-4.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-84 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-121 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-88">

<p style="text-align: justify;">These diagrams demonstrate the fee structure of many property managers including Lifty Life. Lifty Life charges a 25% commission that is not inclusive of third-party fees like the fees of Airbnb or VRBO. In addition, Lifty Life charges a cleaning fee directly to the guest. As you can see the cleaning fee is a fixed rate and is, therefore, a larger portion of the reservation value on smaller bookings.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-85 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-122 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-89">

<h4 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>3. Recurring Expenses</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Among your recurring expenses are anything that has a consistent monthly or annual cost. These expense include utilities, subscriptions, insurance, licensing, banking fees, financing, and strata fees.</p>




<blockquote>


<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: var(--testimonial_bg_color); font-style: normal;"><b>7. Utilities</b></span><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><b style="font-style: normal;"> – </b><span style="font-style: normal;">unlike with long term rentals, as the homeowner, you will be responsible for providing heat, water, electricity, and internet.</span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>8. Subscriptions </b><span style="font-size: 19px;" data-fusion-font="true"><b>– </b>this category includes subscriptions to streaming services (Netflix, Disney+), <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/airbnb-vacation-rental-software/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">vacation rental software</a> (channel manager, dynamic pricing), and business tools (G-suite, accounting software).</span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>9. Insurance – </b>STR insurance is different</span><span style="font-style: normal;"> than your home or rental insurance; </span><span style="font-style: normal;">get a quote on <a href="https://www.squareone.ca/?offer_code=LIFTYLIFE" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">STR insurance here</a>. Not all providers insure short term rentals.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>10. Licensing &#038; Property Taxes – </b>STR licensing can range from $100 to $2500 annually, depending on the city. Property taxes are disclosed on MLS listings.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong style="font-style: normal;">11. Financing &#038; Banking – </strong><span style="font-style: normal;">use a mortgage calculator to get an estimate on your financing costs; <a href="https://www.rbcroyalbank.com/mortgages/mortgage-calculators.html">here is the RBC calculator</a>. Banking expenses include a credit card, chequing account, and e-transfer fees (used to pay cleaners).</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong style="font-style: normal;">12. Strata Fees – </strong><span style="font-style: normal;">in stratified complexes you will also be responsible for strata fees. Check what is included in your strata fees in some cases utilities will be covered. You can find the monthly strata fee on the MLS.</span></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-86 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-123 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-90">

<h4 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 18; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 18;" data-fontsize="18" data-lineheight="30.06px"><b>4. Maintenance</b></h4>




<p style="text-align: justify;">A budget should be set aside for the general maintenance of your property, furnishings, and major amenities such as hot tubs and pools. In addition consider your landscaping and snow removal needs.</p>




<blockquote>


<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><b style="font-style: normal;">13. Handywork &#038; Trades Work – </b><span style="font-style: normal;">it’s a matter of time till you will need some handy or trades work completed. My general rule is to set aside $2 per sqft a year.</span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>14. Landscaping &#038; Snow Removal </b><span style="font-size: 19px;" data-fusion-font="true"><b>– </b>if you are not in a strata building someone will need to support you with landscaping and snow removal. Get quotes from local contractors.</span></span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong style="font-style: normal;">15. Pools &#038; Hot Tubs</strong><span style="font-style: normal;"> – </span><span data-fusion-font="true"><a style="font-size: 19px; font-style: normal;" href="https://alpinecredits.ca/cost-of-swimming-pool/#:~:text=Additionally%2C%20homeowners%20spend%20between%2010,%243%2C000%20to%20maintain%20each%20year." target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pools cost on average $2,000 to $3,000 to maintain</a><span style="font-size: 19px; font-style: normal;">. <a href="https://www.familyhandyman.com/article/how-much-does-a-hot-tub-cost/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Hot tubs cost about $700 to maintain</a>. This assumes you do the work yourself, <span style="font-style: normal;"><span style="font-size: 19px;" data-fusion-font="true">grab quotes from contractors in the area for a quote on their service.</span></span></span></span></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-87 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-124 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-88 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-125 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-91">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>How are Vacation Rentals Valued?</strong></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Now that you’ve narrowed your search to a property plus forecasted revenue and expenses, how do you value the real estate?</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Short term rentals and vacation rentals are still typically valued in the same way as residential real estate. This means that commercial and multi-family real estate metrics such as capitalization (cap) rates aren’t regularly used to value short term rentals. Market comparables and qualitative criteria are the more commonly used to determine asking and offer prices.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-89 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-126 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-92">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Capitalization (Cap) Rates</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Cap rates are a common metric used in real estate investing to calculate the value of an asset. Cap rates are a great tool to identify real estate opportunities. Use this <a href="https://www.omnicalculator.com/finance/cap-rate">Cap Rate Calculator</a> to evaluate the opportunity of your property.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In the long term rental industry a 4 – 12% cap rate is considered good. However what makes a good cap rate varies depending on the market and property type.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-90 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">
