<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-129 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-94">

<blockquote style="text-align: justify;">


<p><span style="font-style: normal;"><b>Pro Tip</b>: calculate if the property would be profitable as a long term rental. As Covid has proven the income of short term rentals is not guaranteed. Have a back up plan in case of the unexpected. Be conservative in your estimates, don’t overleverage, or carry unmanageable risk.</span></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-92 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-130 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-95">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Market Comparables</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Short-term rental real estate is determined primarily by market comparables (comps). Comps are properties that are for sale or have sold that are similar and in the same market. To determine what real estate market comparables to use I’ve compiled a list of quantitative and qualitative criteria to use.</p>




<blockquote style="text-align: justify;">


<p><strong style="font-style: normal;">Real Estate Comps Criteria:</strong></p>




<ul>


<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Square footage (sqft) or square meters (m²)</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Number of bedrooms and bathrooms</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Age of building</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Zoning<br /></span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Building amenities (pools, hot tubs, etc)</span></li>


</ul>


</blockquote>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In most cases you will not find exact matches. Work to create a comp set as similar as possible. In doing so you’ll be able to better identify undervalued or overvalued short-term rental properties.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In addition to creating a market comp for the real estate; you may also want to create a comp of Airbnb listings. Here are some additional criteria to use when creating a comp set for the Airbnb potential.</p>




<blockquote>


<p><b style="font-style: normal;">Airbnb Listings Comps Criteria</b></p>




<ul>


<li><span style="font-style: normal;">Everything from “Real Estate Comps Criteria”</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Furnishings &#038; finishing’s</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Number of reviews and review score</span></li>




<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Average nightly rate and occupancy</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">Number of beds and maximum occupancy</span></li>


</ul>


</blockquote>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Tools like <a href="https://airdna.grsm.io/kwc0oyv7pplw">Airdna’s Rentalizer</a>, example shown below, can also be helpful in quickly identifying an Airbnb comp set.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-93 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-131 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-22 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1258" height="804" alt="Airdna Market Comps" title="Airdna Market Comps" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21141" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153-200x128-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153-400x256-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153-600x383-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153-800x511-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153-1200x767-1.png 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Screenshot-2022-08-28-121153.png 1258w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-94 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-132 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-96">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Qualitative Criteria</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">There are things to value and consider outside of the numbers. Lifty Life for example has market selection criteria that includes things like brand fit and a coolness factor that is unique to our business.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">On the individual investor perspective you should consider how much you or your family will use the property. How well does the lifestyle of the market fit with your own? Does the design and finishing’s of the property fit with your own sense of design? Will you love owning this property? Will this space provide an amazing guest experience?</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-95 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-133 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-97">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Opportunity Costs &#038; Risk</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The final thing to consider when evaluating real estate is to consider the opportunity cost and risk. Does purchasing this property stretch you to aggressively? Would you have a better return on your investment elsewhere? Would it be better to wait till you are in a stronger financial position? Are you fully aware of the risks associated with short term rental investing?</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-96 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-134 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-97 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-135 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-98">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><strong>How can I Finance a Vacation Rental?</strong></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The main ways that short term rentals are financed are through a mortgage from a smaller bank, using a HELOC, and/or pooling resources together through a joint venture. Other financing options that may also be possible is owner financing and commercial lending.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-98 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-136 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-99">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Mortgages</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Mortgages are the most the common way to finance vacation rentals especially for first investment properties. However many major banks such as RBC will not finance short term rentals. The best thing to do is approach a mortgage brokers to get assistance in finding a suitable lender for the property you are interested in. Smaller banks often have more relaxed lending criteria and may be more able to help you.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The other restriction to mortgages can often be the zoning and/or title type. Lots of great properties may be difficult or impossible because of the title. Leaseholds and co-ops are both ownership types that can be difficult to finance with a mortgage.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-99 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-137 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-100">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Home Equity Line of Credit</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">If you already own a home you may have a great source of financing available to you through your Home Equity Line of Credit (HELOC). HELOCs are an amazing financial instrument because of their relatively easy lending restrictions and flexibility.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">With a HELOC you can access the equity of your home, up to 85%. Many short term rentals are purchased with the use of a HELOC on a primary residency. Subsequently many second or third investments are financed from HELOC of the first short term rental investment.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-100 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-138 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-101">

<p style="text-align: justify;">For example since purchasing my first STR in Whistler in 2014 I’ve used years of appreciation to refinance, with a HELOC, and purchase subsequent properties in Canmore and Calgary, Alberta. After closing with the use of a HELOC, I returned to the bank the next day, and converted the HELOC into a mortgage at a lower interest rate.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-139 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-23 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2046" height="1365" alt="The Spruce - Calgary" title="The Spruce – Calgary" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-21124" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005-800x534-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005-1200x801-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/5-603-15-ave-SW-Calgary-2022-0005.jpg 2046w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>



<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-102">

<p style="text-align: center;">Calgary 2 bed townhome “<a href="https://vacation.liftylife.ca/listings/102998" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">The Spruce</a>” purchased in 2022</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-101 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-140 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-103">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Joint Ventures</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Finding investment partners is a fantastic way to access additional capital, lending capacity, and experience. Joint ventures can also mitigate risk by spreading it among more people and forces you to make more calculated decisions that are less influenced by emotion.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Make sure the partner has the same goals as you. If this is a purely an investment all parties should be on board with that. It will cause conflict if one partner is planning on using peak rental dates for personal use and the other wants to maximize earnings by renting the peak season full-time. The best way to resolve these conflicts is to be on the same page from the beginning and to stay in communication about each others plans. You may realize over time your goals may have changed and your expectations departed.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In addition to understanding each others goals make sure to outline each parties responsibilities. Who is gonna be responsible to manage reservations? Who will be managing the cleaning and maintenance of the vacation home? How will the income of the property be split? Who will be on title? Make things are crystal clear from the beginning and consider signing a contract.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-102 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-141 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-103 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-142 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-104">

<h2 class="" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>Where can I find a Knowledgeable STR Realtor?</b></h2>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-104 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-143 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-105">

<p style="text-align: justify;">If you’ve identified some attractive markets, gained an understanding of the opportunity and your financing you are probably ready to reach out to a realtor. But how can you identity a quality realtor with an in-depth knowledge of the short term rental market? It’s not easy because nearly every realtor will say they are experts. We’ve compiled a list of questions to ask realtors to help vet them.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-105 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-144 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-106">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>Questions to Ask Realtors</b></h3>




<blockquote>


<ol>


<li><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-weight: var(--body_typography-font-weight); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); font-style: normal;">Do you own a short-term rental yourself? Have you in the past?</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">How regularly do you help short-term rental investors?</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">What are the restrictions on short-term rentals in your market?</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">How has the market been for short-term rentals been?</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">What are the short-term rental restrictions in {building}?</span></li>




<li><span style="font-style: normal;">Can you recommend a reputable STR management company?</span></li>


</ol>


</blockquote>




<p>A good strategy to vet a realtor is to already have the answer to question 3.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-106 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-145 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-107">

<h3><b>Realtor Referrals</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Among the best strategies to find reputable and qualified realtors is to find recommendations from Airbnb hosts or vacation rental managers.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Lifty Life has a network of realtors which we refer and use personally. We are always happy to <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/contact/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">recommend our network</a>.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-146 fusion_builder_column_1_2 1_2 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:50%;--awb-margin-top-large:94px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.84%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.84%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-24 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="1280" height="916" alt="STR For Sale" title="STR For Sale" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280.png" class="img-responsive wp-image-21057" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280-200x143-1.png 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280-400x286-1.png 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280-600x429-1.png 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280-800x573-1.png 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280-1200x859-1.png 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/house-g53e1ec821_1280.png 1280w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 400px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-107 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-147 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-108 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-148 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-108">

<h2><strong>How to Manage Existing Reservations</strong></h2>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-109 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-149 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-109">

<p style="text-align: justify;">If you are buying an existing short term rental that has future reservations, you may be wondering what to do with the bookings. There are four options to consider but before making a choice you should first do a little analysis.</p>




<ol>


<li style="text-align: justify;">Are the reservations booked at a rate that you feel comfortable honouring? Many owners underprice their units because they manage part-time and/or rely on the Airbnb Smart Pricing algorithm.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Are the Airbnb and VRBO accounts SuperHost and/or Premier Host? How are the reviews?</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Does the property have immediate maintenance or renovation needs that you’d like to address?</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Do some of the booked dates conflict with dates you’d like to use the property personally?</li>


</ol>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Once you’ve answered if the reservations are worth keeping and whether or not the accounts are in good standing you can consider one of four strategies to deal with existing reservations.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-110 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-150 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-110">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>1. Taking Over Accounts</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The first option to consider is taking over the Airbnb and VRBO accounts of the previous owner. This is only sensible if the accounts have lots of high-quality reviews and/or are SuperHost/Premier Host. I recommend against this option but many buyers choose to go down this route since it can provide a lot of value and creditability.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-111 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-151 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="accordian fusion-accordian" style="--awb-border-size:1px;--awb-icon-size:16px;--awb-content-font-size:20px;--awb-icon-alignment:right;--awb-hover-color:#f9f9f9;--awb-border-color:#cccccc;--awb-background-color:#ffffff;--awb-divider-color:#e0dede;--awb-divider-hover-color:#e0dede;--awb-icon-color:#0f7375;--awb-title-color:#0288ef;--awb-content-color:#000000;--awb-icon-box-color:#333333;--awb-toggle-hover-accent-color:#0f7375;--awb-title-font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;--awb-title-font-weight:400;--awb-title-font-style:normal;--awb-title-font-size:18px;--awb-content-font-family:"Questrial";--awb-content-font-style:normal;--awb-content-font-weight:400;">

<div class="panel-group fusion-toggle-icon-right fusion-toggle-icon-boxed" id="accordion-21024-1">

<div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-3e727b1f3097b5b19 fusion-toggle-has-divider">

<div class="panel-heading">

<h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_3e727b1f3097b5b19"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="3e727b1f3097b5b19" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#3e727b1f3097b5b19" href="#3e727b1f3097b5b19"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">The Steps to taking over Airbnb/VRBO accounts:</span></a></h4>

</div>



<div id="3e727b1f3097b5b19" class="panel-collapse collapse " araia-labelledby="toggle_3e727b1f3097b5b19">

<div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">


<ol>


<li style="text-align: justify;">Discuss account transfer with the current owner. In many cases, the owner may not approve this because they don’t feel comfortable or they have other listings on the account. If they will allow account transfer that’s great! Move onto step two.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Determine the date that existing reservations should be paid to the new owner. The most sensible date is the occupancy date.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Make sure to have any deposits already paid out by guests transferred to you. Guests may have paid a deposit to the current owner in reservations from VRBO, Booking.com, direct reservations, and others. In some cases, Airbnb reservations may have also already been paid to the owner so ask about that as well.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Replace any profile details on the account with your own. This includes names, the profile photos, emails, phone numbers, and the profile description.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Remove any unwanted cohosts from the account.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Delete and replace bank or payout details with your own.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Delete and replace any payment details such as credit card details from the traveler section.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Remove any attached third-party accounts such as channel managers, dynamic pricing, etc.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Inform existing guests of the change in property ownership and any other changes you will be making to the property or listing.</li>


</ol>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-112 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-152 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-111">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>2. Rebooking Guests onto your Accounts</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Assuming the reservations have been booked at reasonable rates and the dates work for your needs the best option is to rebook guests onto your own account. This is Lifty Life’s preferred strategy because it keeps guests happy, guarantees income, and builds up the review base on your personal accounts.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-113 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-153 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="accordian fusion-accordian" style="--awb-border-size:1px;--awb-icon-size:16px;--awb-content-font-size:20px;--awb-icon-alignment:right;--awb-hover-color:#f9f9f9;--awb-border-color:#cccccc;--awb-background-color:#ffffff;--awb-divider-color:#e0dede;--awb-divider-hover-color:#e0dede;--awb-icon-color:#0f7375;--awb-title-color:#0288ef;--awb-content-color:#000000;--awb-icon-box-color:#333333;--awb-toggle-hover-accent-color:#0f7375;--awb-title-font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;--awb-title-font-weight:400;--awb-title-font-style:normal;--awb-title-font-size:18px;--awb-content-font-family:"Questrial";--awb-content-font-style:normal;--awb-content-font-weight:400;">

<div class="panel-group fusion-toggle-icon-right fusion-toggle-icon-boxed" id="accordion-21024-2">

<div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-b50363462a4511990 fusion-toggle-has-divider">

<div class="panel-heading">

<h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_b50363462a4511990"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="b50363462a4511990" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#b50363462a4511990" href="#b50363462a4511990"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">The Steps to Rebooking Guests onto your Accounts:</span></a></h4>

</div>



<div id="b50363462a4511990" class="panel-collapse collapse " araia-labelledby="toggle_b50363462a4511990">

<div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">


<ol>


<li style="text-align: justify;">Ask the current owner about already paid deposits for future reservations. Make sure these funds are transferred to you. If not, don’t honour the reservation and have the current owner cancel the reservations on their account and at their expense.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Have the current owner stop taking on new reservations.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">If you don’t already have an account on Airbnb/VRBO create an account.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Create listings on these sites that guests can book on.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Closeout availability for the dates already booked so you don’t accidentally double-book</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Have the current owner of the account update guests on the change. If there are going to be any changes in the unit such as furnishings, price, or policies let them know at this time.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Give the owner your Airbnb/VRBO URLs so that he can provide them to guests. Guests will need to cancel their current reservations and rebook on the new account.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Provide guests with the option to cancel their reservations if they are uncomfortable with the changes.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Airbnb guests should be provided the Airbnb listing. VRBO guests should be provided the VRBO listing. Do not make this an opportunity to rebook guests onto another site or with you directly.</li>


</ol>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-114 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-154 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-112">

<h3 class="" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>3. Canceling Reservations</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">If for whatever reason you don’t want to honour the existing reservations; having the current owner cancel reservations is the best option. You have no obligation to honour any booking made by the current owner or by their management company. This strategy is likely to be the most contentious between buyer, seller, and perhaps management company.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Canceling bookings is the simplest strategy on your end. The only thing you’ll need to do is alert the seller that you won’t be honouring existing reservations. It will be on the owner to cancel reservations with guests, provide refunds, and deal with the consequences. The one step you should take to minimize risk is to replace the door codes and/or locks.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-115 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-155 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-113">

<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b>4. Keeping them as a Cohost</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The final and least common strategy is to contract the current owner as a cohost or property manager. This strategy is only sensible if the seller has been a strong operator that you believe will continue to provide a great service. Ask the seller about this option. If they are interested consider signing a contract, determine the revenue split, and get yourself cohosted on the listings. This is a great strategy for a passive investor.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Alternatively</span> if the current owner is using a vacation rental manager consider contracting with that management organization to continue managing your unit.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-116 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-156 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;">

<div class="fusion-separator-border sep-double" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#e0dede;border-top-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-117 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-157 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-114">

<h2><strong>Should I Hire a Vacation Rental Management Company?</strong></h2>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-118 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-158 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-115">

<p style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 40px; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fusion-font="true">A property manager is a great option if you are investing into short term rentals. With a manager there is no need to take the 4am calls from guests, no need to worry about cleaning, no need to stress about toilet paper, or the hundred other issues that arise when operating a vacation home. For investors looking to remain more passive a short term rental manager is a welcome investment. A good manager will more than make up for their expense by freeing up your time, protecting your asset, and out-preforming the market.</p>

Well, the [&#8230;]</p>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-121 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<span class="awb-title-spacer fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility"></span>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<div style="text-align: center;"><b style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">The 4 Best Remote Work Destinations in BC</b></div>

</h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-122 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-166 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-118">

<p style="text-align: justify;">With the advent of the ‘new normal,’ businesses have not only reevaluated how they operate, but many Canadians have also realized that they would prefer to operate on their own terms, balancing a workweek between locations conducive to their productivity. Well, the fun side of it, who wouldn’t love to work with a great view in a different environment that is not just their wall and boring work desk, right?</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-123 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-167 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-119">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><b style="color: var(--h2_typography-color); font-family: var(--h2_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h2_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h2_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing); text-transform: var(--h2_typography-text-transform); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">What Should You Consider When Planning a Workcation?</b></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Make sure you have enough room to create your own little workstation. For this, you will need to ensure you have a desk and chair to accommodate yourself and your laptop.</p>




<ul>


<li style="text-align: justify;">Ensure you have a strong Wifi connection available</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Verify if the cell-service provided in the area is strong enough</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Choose a more quieter place in order to avoid background noise during meetings and discussions</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">If you are a remote working parent and want to accommodate your children along with you, ensure the destination is children-friendly</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">If you cannot travel to work without your pet, you might as well need to verify if the destination is pet-friendly!</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Pick a more calmer environment. It helps you to stay calm and maintain a more positive mindset throughout your workload.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Check for cafes, restaurants or other eateries that you could benefit from for quick bites and beverages</li>


</ul>




<p style="text-align: justify;">If you are now sure about what you’ll need to look for in remote work destinations in BC, here are 4 best remote work <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/staycation-in-bc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">destinations in BC</a> to inspire you to change your boring routine up!</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-120">

<h2><b>1. Vancouver </b></h2>




<p>The city is currently one of the most desirable work destinations in BC, without a doubt! People spend countless hours behind laptops here in cafes, libraries, public spaces, and on some beaches as well. Free WIFI is available in the hills, and you’ll be able to locate it with no trouble! As a matter of fact, all of the city’s streets are covered in free wifi, which isn’t a secret at all.</p>




<p>Since these are our personal favorite spots, we highly recommend that you work primarily in and around downtown and the West End, including hipster cafes, non-hipster cafes, beaches, and other random public places.</p>




<p>Here’s a list of some of the best places for remote work in Vancouver:</p>




<ul>


<li>Kafka’s Coffee and Tea</li>




<li>Propaganda Coffee</li>




<li>Breka on Bute</li>




<li>Vancouver Central Library</li>




<li>Jim Deva Plaza</li>


</ul>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-171 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-121">

<h2 style="text-align: justify;"><b>2. Penticton </b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">More and more remote workers are choosing to move to Penticton because it offers them easy access to green space, lakes, and recreation. This gives them a better work-life balance and gives them the freedom to do what they love!</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Penticton is a town where you can enjoy life and make a good living at the same time. The town isn’t like any other. The town is where everyone finds their place. The summers are long and hot on the lake, and the winters are mild and dry. Bike tours offer the chance to explore award-winning wineries, world-class trails, and breathtaking views.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Whether you want to start a business or grow your career, Penticton is the place to do it. Because if you are someone who would love to embrace the idea that your home isn’t just where you live, it’s where you make a living, then this is one of the best remote work destinations in BC that you cannot miss!</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">There are many great places to work remotely in this beautiful region, whether you live in it or plan to go there for work. Now you know what to look for as far as remote workplaces are concerned. Oftentimes, change is the only constant in life. Therefore, don’t let boring work memories dampen your work spirits and pick your desired work destination in <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/the-best-places-to-visit-in-bc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">British Columbia</a>!</p>

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-173 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-122">

<h2><b>3. Tofino</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">With beach, surf, and breathtaking outdoors as its backdrop, Tofino is becoming one of the most desirable remote work destinations. This is because it has created a new coworking community that attracts a steady stream of global nomads.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Tofino, despite its thriving community, is seeking to diversify while supporting residents, businesses, and visitors at the same time. On the western coast of Vancouver Island, Tofino is a remote destination for tourists who enjoy nature, play in the waves, and relax by the sea. The town is close enough to the city that you feel removed from big-city hustle and bustle. Despite this, there are plenty of things to do, great accommodations, and fine dining options.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">So, if you are looking for one of the best remote working destinations with a less chaotic environment that you could work from in peace, Tofino is the best pick!</p>


</div>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-174 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-131 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-175 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-123">

<h2 style="text-align: justify;"><b>4. Harrison Hot Springs </b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Known for its urban vibe, natural beauty, and scrumptious dining options, Harrison Hot Springs is far more than Canada’s food capital. In the surrounding areas of this destination, there are a number of hot springs that are capable of leaving visitors in awe. Being home to some of the most stunning natural wonders of the world, along with modern lifestyles, <a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/things-to-do-in-harrison-hot-springs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Harrison Hot Springs</a> appeals to those travelers who are seeking the finest of both worlds.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">For workers desiring an escape into nature away from the bustling city life or boring office walls, Harrison Hot Springs is one of the ideal remote working destinations in BC, ever!</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<h2><b>3. <a href="https://amzn.to/3A3vM7A" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">0 to 500 Properties in 5 Years</a></b></h2>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-139 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >
