<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-185 fusion_builder_column_2_3 2_3 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:66.666666666667%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:2.88%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:2.88%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-130">

<p style="text-align: justify;">0 to 500 Properties is written for the most ambitious short term rental managers. If you are looking to scale your business to hundreds of properties this is a great read. Author, Brooke Pfautz is the CEO of Vintory, a CRM for vacation rentals. The book has some great lessons although it often reads as a sales strategy for Vintory. Regardless there are great lessons in here that were learnt during his time developing Vantage Resort Realty.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-186 fusion_builder_column_1_3 1_3 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:33.333333333333%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:5.76%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:5.76%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<h2><b>2. <a href="0px !important;' />&#8221; target=&#8221;_blank&#8221; rel=&#8221;noopener noreferrer&#8221;>Short-Term Rental Long-Term Wealth</a></b></h2>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-141 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

As such Short-Term Rental Long Term Wealth is published under the Bigger Pockets brand. The book chronicles Avery’s experience investing in vacation rentals within the Smoky Mountains. There is a heavy focus on financial analysis, operational efficiency, and investing. Avery does a great job making these concepts very accessible.</p>

If you are interested in driving more direct business this is a must read.</p>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-195 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-5 fusion-title-text fusion-title-size-one">

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-left fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

<span class="awb-title-spacer fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility"></span>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<div style="text-align: center;"><b style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Banff National Park Ski Resorts | Ultimate Guide</b></div>

</h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-147 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-196 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-137">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It is an unforgettable experience to ski in Banff National Park, an area deeply rooted in the North American culture of skiing. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">There are some excellent skiing opportunities in Banff, and those who ski or ride regularly will definitely have some amazing days. With some amazing ski resorts, a wide variety of accommodation and dining options, wildlife, consistent temperatures, a charming town, and plenty of off-mountain activities, this is the place to go for a memorable skiing experience.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visiting Banff and Canada offers access to some of the </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/bc-mountain-resorts/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">world’s best ski resorts</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> at a relatively low cost. So, we decided to provide you with this ultimate guide to ski resorts within Banff National Park. </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-148 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-197 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-138">

<h2><b>How to Get to Banff National Park</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The journey to Banff National Park isn’t as difficult as you might think. Calgary International Airport has many airlines that offer direct flights. The scenic drive to Banff takes 90 minutes (140 kilometers or 87 miles) from the airport. You can take shuttle buses to Banff and Lake Louise from Calgary International Airport, or you can rent a car in Calgary or at the airport. For those who wish to travel by road, Vancouver International Airport is 850 kilometers (530 miles) away from Banff &#038; Lake Louise.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-149 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-198 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-139">

<h2><b>Tips for Skiing in Banff</b></h2>




<ul>


<li style="text-align: justify;">Plan to visit over the holidays so you won’t have to ski on a busy weekend and will have more time to do other interesting things around town and at the park.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">You can find rentals around town if you need them! There is a wide range of options between Banff, Canmore, and ski resorts.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Those who are not comfortable driving in the snow may want to consider using a private vehicle or the free shuttle bus service. While you don’t need a car, you can still make use of this if you want to visit other sites.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">There might be tracks beyond resort boundaries, but DO NOT cross them without avalanche gear and knowledge of the terrain.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Don’t forget about all the other excellent winter activities Banff has to offer. If you’re visiting for the first time, there are a lot of things to enjoy, regardless of whether you ski or snowboard.</li>




<li style="text-align: justify;">Oh, and make sure to wear warm clothing! Banff has some of the coldest temperatures in North America, and wind chills of -20C aren’t uncommon. This is where layering comes into play. If you get too hot, you can drop a layer.</li>


</ul>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-150 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-199 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-140">

<h2><b>The Complete List of Banff National Park Ski Resorts</b></h2>

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-200 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-201 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-141">

<h3><b>1. Mount Norquay </b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Among Banff’s attractions, <a href="https://banffnorquay.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Mount Norquay</a> is a people pleaser. With a funky family vibe, this local favorite is a hidden gem in Banff National Park. Mt. Norquay’s night skiing is perfect for finding perfect stashes all to yourself on a powder day and ripping up perfect groomers during the day. You can find terrain that will appeal to everyone here, from beginners to advanced skiers.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/where-to-stay-canmore-or-banff/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Located right outside of Banff</a>, Canada’s snow-mad settlement where you can find cozy holiday condos and chalets, plus stores, restaurants, and native wildlife, Mount Norquay is a great place to stay for a vacation.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Snow activities such as sleigh rides, dog sledding, and hiking are also available at Norquay. The ski resort has 60 marked runs, multiple terrain parks, and alternative snow activities such as sledding. Learning to ski or snowboard here is one of the best things you can do in Canada. Approximately 56 percent of runs are designed for beginners and intermediate skiers, and the snow school offers clinics and private lessons for kids and adults.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">There are two dining options on the mountain for those who need to take a break, including the resort’s daycare, which is open from 9 am to 4 pm. The Mountain Host initiative, however, is one of Norquay’s most impressive features. Norquay locals offer tours around the mountain to new visitors so that they can discover the best areas to ski or board. You don’t have to stress about being challenged – Norquay is used for Olympic training and World Cup training.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">For tailgate lunch in the parking lot, Mount Norquay offers several great grab-and-go options, and they offer fresh baked goods every day. Pastries are available at the Cascade Lodge main level cafeteria. Take-out is another great option at Banff, so pick one up to bring along for your parking lot lunch!</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Don’t miss Mt. Norquay’s tubing and skiing at night if you’re visiting during the weekend! Coming in the middle of the week? You can still enjoy tubing every day.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-153 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-202 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-154 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-203 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-142">

<h3><b>2. Sunshine Village </b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><a href="https://www.skibanff.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Sunshine Village</a> offers the longest ski season in Canada and more snow than any of its Banff neighbors. It does not waste any of this incredible snow. You will find more than 1,335 hectares of terrain, including some of the most thrilling runs in the world, including Delirium Dive (voted as one of the top 10 off-piste destinations in the world). There are 50 jibs, rails, boxes, jumps, and tubes included in Rogers Terrain Park, which compliments all this downhill action.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The unique experience of snowboarding or skiing between two Canadian provinces is another reason to visit Sunshine Village during your next snow holiday. You can swerve over to British Columbia while descending Lookout Mountain, then return to Alberta in one trail.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">As Sunshine’s peaks soar well above the treeline, they also provide its visitors with some of the best views in skiing – after perhaps a powder shot.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Even after you’ve unclipped, there’s plenty to keep you busy. A variety of dining options are available, including coffee shops, gourmet dinners around a fire, and lively bars. You can learn about Canadian history and culture on the Historical Snowshoe and Fondue Tour. The Sunshine Mountain Lodge offers the only ski-in ski-out accommodation in Banff as well as regular bonfires, an outdoor hot tub, and tobogganing.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-155 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-204 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-33 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="Lake Louise Resort Skiing" title="Lake Louise Resort Skiing" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20845" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/a17-020256-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-156 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-205 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-143">

<h3><b>3. Lake Louise Ski Resort </b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">The <a href="https://www.skilouise.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Lake Louise Ski Resort</a> has one of the best views of any ski resort around the world. Banff National Park, Canada’s crown jewel, is home to the ski resort, which offers a wealth of natural splendor. Skiing in Banff is second to none!</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In between runs screaming down groomers, or taking on bowls, the park offers fresh air and picturesque views. The long runs in the valley forest, which snake down from the alpine, are another option for skiers not looking for thrills. Many travelers have been inspired by the craggy peaks and forested valleys.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Regardless of skill level, Lake Louise Ski Resort has something to offer everyone. This ski resort happens to be one of our favorites worldwide and offers many attractions for visitors. The Lake Louise Ski Resort should be on the bucket list of every avid skier and snowboarder.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-206 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-158 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-207 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-144">

<h3><b>4. Nakiska Ski Resort </b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Located in the beautiful Kananaskis Country, <a href="https://skinakiska.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Nakiska Ski Resort</a> offers a family-friendly ski resort. In the Canadian Rockies, this ski resort has a rich history, a convenient location, and terrain that will appeal to all ages and abilities.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">This ski resort is located on the traditional territory of three indigenous people groups: Stoney, Tsuut’ina, and Ktunaxa. Named for the Indigenous peoples whose land it is, the ski resort honors their culture and heritage.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Nakiska is not only a 50-minute drive from Banff and 35-minutes from Canmore, but is also competitive with some other Canadian ski resorts such as Lake Louise and Banff Sunshine.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Being within such close proximity to the main cities and towns of the area, Nakiska provides a comforting feeling of belonging. There are many families and friends who have enjoyed Nakiska Ski Resort and have been together for many years. This resort has large mountains that tend to attract most tourists and hardcore skiers. Children and teens tearing up the slopes with friends, toddlers learning from their parents, and whole families shredding together is a fun sight to see!</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">This resort is ideally situated for locals, but guests should not miss the breathtaking views as well! There are impressive mountains all around you no matter where you are on the ski hill.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">For beginners, Nakiska offers an ideal location to learn to ski on a smaller, more manageable hill, while still enjoying the mountains that are characteristic of the Canadian Rockies.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">It’s not just that you can enjoy great family skiing at this mountain, but it also offers activities off skis. It is difficult to get bored here since there are snow tubing hills and snowshoeing trails.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">It is impossible not to be enchanted by the Wanidu Tube Park at Nakiska. All you need is a thrill-seeking attitude and some warm clothes, as they provide you with tubes and a push down the hill. You can use this as a way to enjoy the mountain air with friends or family while you’re off the skis.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">Then there are Nakiska’s stunning snowshoeing trails, in case skiing and snow tubing are not enough. Their website allows you to book guided tours and pick up rentals when you arrive. Beginners, intermediates, and advanced hikers can all enjoy the surrounding mountains on their trails! Booking your tour in advance will ensure availability.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">There are some days when the best part of the ski day is eating lunch with your friends! On snowy days, though, lunch is just a quick refueling stop before continuing on with the fun in the mountains. Regardless of the type of day you’re having, Nakiska Ski Resort offers food for everyone.</p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">In addition to several restaurants, there is a café, a barbecue pit, and an area where you can eat your packed lunch at Nakiska Ski Resort. There is a wide variety of comfort foods available on their menus to keep you warm during a chilly day. During a nice day, be sure to enjoy a meal on their balcony while soaking up the sun and taking in the views.</p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>




<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.liftylife.ca/banff-national-park-ski-resorts/">Banff National Park Ski Resorts | Ultimate Guide</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.liftylife.ca">Lifty Life</a>.</p>

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-6 fusion-title-text fusion-title-size-one">

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-left fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

<span class="awb-title-spacer fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility"></span>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<div style="text-align: center;"><strong style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">The 10 Hidden Gem Destinations of BC</strong></div>

</h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-209 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-145">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It’s no secret that the </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/trip-to-the-canadian-rockies/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Rocky Mountains</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/things-to-do-in-whistler/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Whistler</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, and Victoria are world-renowned tourism destinations in western Canada. Each year, millions visit these cities and towns for good reasons. But, what if we tell you that you are missing out on many more? Here’s a list of 10 hidden gem </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/the-best-places-to-visit-in-bc/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">destinations of BC</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> that you may have never known or visited before! </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><span><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">You may be wondering, “OKA-WHAT?” or be asking “HOW DID I NOT-” Well, you’re not alone! These are unknown places to many people from British </span></span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Columbia</span><span><span style="font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing); color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">. Hopefully you you are a fan of incredible hot springs, breathtaking scenery, world-class wineries, and desert exploration.</span></span></span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-160 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-210 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-35 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="mountains in british columbia" title="mountains in british columbia" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20637" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/trevor-mckinnon-ALTWTTtYz5Y-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-161 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-211 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-146">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>1. Ancient Cedars Loop – Ucluelet</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">As you hike along the </span><a href="https://www.wildpacifictrail.com/map.html"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Wild Pacific Trail</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, you are like walking through a living piece of art. There isn’t a place like it on </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">Vancouver</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Island that is so awe-inspiring and dramatic that you feel the power of nature and of the sea!</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">A junction for the </span><a href="https://www.alltrails.com/trail/canada/british-columbia/ancient-cedars-loop"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Ancient Cedars Loop </span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">is located just before the 7 km marker on the Wild Pacific Trail. This trail is one km long and is shaded by ancient and giant cedars that tower overhead. These trees are over 800 years old!</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">As one of the hidden gems in BC, a walk along the Ancient Cedars Loop provides you with the opportunity to see old-growth Sitka spruces, western hemlocks, and giant red cedars (the oldest trees on the Ucluelet peninsula). One behemoth measures over 12 meters around its base, and two are estimated to be over 800 years old. Since cedars have natural hollows, it is difficult to determine their exact ages. As this ancient specimen falls, it clearly exhibits countless rings – imagine the thunder it created as it fell. Taking a walk through the cedars you can reflect on what they have endured – gale-force winds, lightning strikes, and perhaps even a tsunami 300 years ago. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It features untouched examples of giant nurse-logs, raised root systems, mosses, fungi, lichens, and ferns, as well as a hand-hewn path through old-growth rainforest. The opportunity to capture close-up images of rainforest delights will be especially appealing to photographers.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-162 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-212 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-36 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1683" alt="green forests" title="green forests" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20638" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-200x132-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-400x263-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-600x395-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-800x526-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-1200x789-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-T5w1xkN1c-Q-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-163 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-213 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-147">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>2. Free Spirit Spheres – Qualicum Beach</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">As you sway side-to-side, you can see trees and leaves in all directions. The smells of the forest will fill your senses as you take deep breaths. Free Spirit Spheres will definitely evoke childhood memories of climbing and treehouses. There will be no roughing it here, this is the grown-up version. </span><a href="https://freespiritspheres.com/directions/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free Spirit Spheres</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> can provide you with tranquility and even luxury if you’re looking for a change of pace from trails and campgrounds.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Cedar and spruce balls recall huge nuts and seeds and work in cooperation with the natural environment. By attaching the suspension to a number of strong points among the trees, it mimics spider webs.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In addition to making use of sailboats and construction methods heavily, the spheres are made of wood and fiberglass. There are fold-out tables and mirrors inside the curving walls as well as curved benches and beds and tiny appliances hidden inside the portholes.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The free spirit spheres can be rented overnight for those seeking “the ultimate tree-house experience.” For a look-see, you must book an appointment since they are on private property. </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-164 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-214 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-37 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="free spirit island" title="free spirit island" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20639" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/andrew-svk-v8lOJWSnZqo-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-165 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-215 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-148">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>3. Othello Tunnels – Hope</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">As a part of the historic Kettle Valley Railway, the Othello Tunnels are located near Hope, B.C. These tunnels were built in 1914 and have an interesting history. The railway ceased operation in 1961. It is this section of the railway that has become Coquihalla Canyon Provincial Park since 1986.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><a href="https://youtu.be/bjfimxkb460"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Othello Tunnels</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> are among the masterpieces of early 1900s engineering. The canyon’s geology and the tunnels’ inventive engineering make it a popular tourist destination. Through steep canyon walls, there are 5 tunnels that make up the Othello Tunnels. Coquihalla River snakes thunderously through the canyon below, passing beneath two trestles connecting the tunnels.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The tunnels can be explored in two ways. One option is to follow the tunnels straight from the parking lot and return after passing through all of them. You can do this short hike if you’re short on time or have small children if you’re limited on time.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Alternatively, you can hike the Hope-Nicola Valley Trail. You will traverse a scenic forest for 6 km, with some good climbing. Afterward, the loop ends by returning through the Othello Tunnels.</span></p>




<blockquote>


<p><b>Did you know? </b></p>




<p><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Othello Tunnels were named after the famous character from the play Othello. It is because the engineer of the tunnels, McCulloch, was a big fan of Shakespeare! </span></i></p>


</blockquote>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-166 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-216 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-38 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1710" alt="tunnel in canada" title="tunnel in canada" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20640" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-200x134-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-600x401-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-800x534-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-1200x802-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/karsten-winegeart-oladJqxWqyg-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-167 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-217 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-149">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>4. The Tree on the Lake – Port Renfrew</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">For those who may look at this title and wonder, what could be so unique about a tree on the lake? Here’s what you need to know! </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In the calm waters of Fairy Lake on Vancouver Island, 70 miles from the port city of Victoria on </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/the-best-places-to-visit-in-bc/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">British Columbia’s coast</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, is a plucky arboreal wonder.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The idyllic Fairy Lake is located in the unspoiled landscape of Port Renfrew, living up to its name. Against the stillness of the lake, a submerged log stands out. The Douglas fir tree is clinging to the log with all its might. Moreover, this log, too, is made of Douglas fir. The dead tree provided the stunted tree with food and support, so it’s as though it sacrificed itself to the tiny tree that grew on it. There are many tourists, boaters, and hikers that come to enjoy this unique view of nature and rebirth. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Among the reasons this tree is so popular is that it requires no hiking to see it as it can easily be seen from the edge of Pacific Marine Road. If you’d like to find the exact location, you can use Google Maps, although, keep in mind that there is no cell service out here. Therefore, download area maps in advance so that you can use them offline.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-168 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-218 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-39 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="2048" alt="port renfrew" title="port renfrew" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20641" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-200x160-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-400x320-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-600x480-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-800x640-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-1200x960-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/faye-cornish-Uq3gTiPlqRo-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>
