<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-169 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-219 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-150">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>5. Parkhurst Ghost Village – Whistler</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">On the shores of </span><a href="https://landwithoutlimits.com/places/land-of-hidden-waters/green-lake/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Green Lake</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> sits an abandoned logging settlement filled with historical artifacts including crumbled buildings, abandoned cars, old stoves, and even a cabin. There has been no one in the town since the 1960s, and the forest is gradually reclaiming the land.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">For an experience that is off the beaten track, try hiking to the Parkhurst Ghost Town in Whistler.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;"> The trail is usually free of snow between April and October. Between December and March, you’ll need snowshoes and good route-finding skills. The call is yours when you want to take the trip! </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once you’ve decided when you want to go, here’s more you’ll need to know. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The small settlement was home to about 70 loggers. A store and school were built in the late 1930s, but they did not last long. Today, some rusting buildings and vehicles remain. Over 70 loggers lived and worked in the small settlement, which has been covered in colorful graffiti. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Best hiking trail with a lot of spooky and unique discoveries, the Parkhurst Ghost Town in Whistler is for adventure-seekers and thrillers! </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-170 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-220 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-40 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="ghost village canada" title="ghost village canada" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20642" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/dan-meyers-m4FB7fzTr80-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-171 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-221 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-151">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>6. The Spotted Lake – Osoyoos</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">According to the British Columbia Visitor Centre, </span><a href="https://mapcarta.com/24653636"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Spotted Lake</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> has been considered sacred by the indigenous people of the Okanagan Nation for centuries. According to them, each of the circles was reputed to have healing and medicinal properties. Indigenous peoples of the Okanagan Valley called it Kliluk Lake.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">Although it may look all fairytale for some, spooky for others, you can’t get too close to the lake if you want to see it. With a sign explaining that the area is culturally and ecologically sensitive, a fence has been erected to protect it. The polka dots on the lake, however, can be viewed from various vantage points along the highway.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-172 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-222 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-152">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>7. Smiling Buddha Room – Horne Lake</b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It’s not hard at all to spot the image of Buddha sitting serenely above a reflecting pool in one of the caves known as the “smiling buddha room.”. A reflection of the Buddha’s form is mirrored in the pool, creating an incredibly beautiful image.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Those taking part in caving adventures are always surprised by what they find. In a cave full of beauty, Buddha makes a picture that’s sure to make it onto Instagram.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Aside from hidden waterfalls, ancient fossils, crystalline formations and so much more, island caving is truly a unique and exciting experience. </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-173 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-223 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-41 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="lake view in british columbia" title="lake view in british columbia" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20643" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/joel-mott-kMwVHtKcGnQ-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-174 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-224 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-153">

<p> <b style="color: var(--h2_typography-color); font-family: var(--h2_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h2_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h2_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">8. Greenheart Treewalk – Vancouver</b></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">A canopy walkway, Greenheart TreeWalk provides an aerial trail that allows visitors to experience the forest from an elevated vantage point. By exploring this lofty environment, visitors can learn about its flora and fauna.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">A 310 meter-long treetop canopy walkway, located in the center of </span><a href="https://botanicalgarden.ubc.ca/files/2015/12/ubc-botancial-garden-map-2015_final.pdf"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UBC Botanical Garden</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, is hung from massive Douglas fir, cedar, and grand fir trees, some of which are over 100 years old. The walkway offers a bird’s eye view of Vancouver’s amazing coastal temperate rainforest from nearly 20 meters in height. As you navigate suspended walkways and tree platforms high above the forest floor, your adventurous spirit is sure to be sparked. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Walk from one platform to the next at your own pace or opt for an informative tour led by knowledgeable guides. On a viewing platform 23 meters above the forest floor, you will be able to take in the sights and sounds as if you’re 23 meters above the forest floor.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">With Greenheart’s approach, trees and habitats are impacted in the smallest possible way. A treetop canopy walkway system that is bolted into the trees can damage the trees or the delicate ecosystem surrounding them. However, the Greenheart TreeWalk does not damage trees or surrounding ecosystems. The platforms are hung from trees by an innovative cable tension system, removing the need for nails and bolts. With features like the “Tree Hugger” cable system and the “Kissing Bar”, the walkway is an excellent addition to the forest’s landscape.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-175 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-225 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-42 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="greenheart treewalk" title="greenheart treewalk" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20644" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/james-youn-9HqUHlzfHms-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-176 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-226 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-154">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>9. Angel Springs – Kelowna </b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">This moderate trail in </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/things-to-do-in-kelowna/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Kelowna</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> begins at Little White Forestry Service Road and offers visitors a chance to see natural springs and interesting geological formations.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Located along KLO creek, the trail is 4km long and has narrative plaques that describe the local flora, including Douglas-fir, Lodgepole Pine, Western Larch, and Western Red Cedar.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Even though the underground water is heated to over 100°C through geothermal action, the surface springs are lukewarm at about 25°C and can be recognized by tufa deposits that are orange in color and higher than a meter high. The mineral tuff is formed when calcite crystallizes after evaporating water.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">During springtime, Angel Springs can become quite cool from mountain runoff. For best results, visit in the summer.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-177 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-227 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-155">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>10. Spirit Trail – Harrison Hot Springs </b></h2>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The story behind the </span><a href="https://www.google.com/maps/place/Spirit+Trail/@49.2844506,-121.7795527,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m5!3m4!1s0x548413c8533ad091:0x28fb8bbfed84c031!8m2!3d49.2844506!4d-121.777364"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Spirit Trail </span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">captures our attention. Following his walk through the woods with his dog, an artist created clay masks for trees. He believed that “the woods were enchanted and that the trees had individual personalities.”</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It is very easy to walk the Spirit Trail. It’s a beautiful trail full of ferns and fun little spots to explore along its length. </span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">At the end of the trail, there is a group of masks arranged in a circle. You feel as if they are staring at you from every angle. A haunting and enchanting experience, yet almost eerie and haunting at the same time.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The 30-minute walk through the lush and scenic cedar forest is short and sweet. A short drive from </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/destinations/harrison-hot-springs-vacation-rentals/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Harrison Hot Springs</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> brings you to the trailhead, where you can easily get in touch with nature.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-178 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-228 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-43 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="harrison hot springs" title="harrison hot springs" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20645" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/jorge-ramirez-ZjBcdSVQctg-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-179 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-229 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-156">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Well, now you can say goodbye to your usual trips around B.C and set your bucket list goals to check out these 10 hidden gems of B.C! Don’t waste any more time, add them all to your list right away and start exploring. </span></p>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-180 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-230 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-7 fusion-title-text fusion-title-size-one">

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-left fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

<span class="awb-title-spacer fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility"></span>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;">

<h1><b>How to Brew Coffee While Camping </b></h1>

</h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-231 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-157">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Camping, the always popular </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/bc-bucket-list/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">outdoor recreational activity</span></a>,<span style="font-weight: 400;"> is a great way to get away from your regular life and just enjoy days in the wild.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">It takes time for camping enthusiasts to get accustomed to their new surroundings. So it is fair to say that most of them miss their regular coffee while on the campground. They usually rely on regular coffee makers which are not designed for outdoor use or instant coffee. But if you want to brew your favorite cup of joe while camping, there are some easy ways to do it like using a <a href="https://stormandswell.ca/how-to-make-french-press-coffee/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">French press</a> or instant coffee packets.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0); color: var(--body_typography-color); font-family: var(--body_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--body_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--body_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--body_typography-letter-spacing);">However, there are many other ways to brew coffee while camping, and we will share with you some of the easiest ways to brew coffee while camping!</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-181 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-232 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-233 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-158">

<p><b>Preparation: </b></p>




<ul>


<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consider the size and weight of your coffee utensils and ingredients (particularly if backpacking) </span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Know well about your expected group size </span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Rehearse your speed (who’s the quickest coffee maker?) </span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Know easy cleanup methods </span></li>


</ul>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Now, to 5 of the best ways to make coffee while camping (proven!). </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-183 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-234 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-159">

<h2><b>1. Brew Steeped Coffee or Specialty Instant Coffee</b></h2>




<ul>


<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It will take you 30 seconds to 4 minutes (depending on your speed!) </span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">What you’ll need is: instant coffee, a kettle, and water</span></li>


</ul>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It’s actually a good idea to carry </span><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Nescafe-classic-CASE-28-18g/dp/B006WAJKL2/ref=sr_1_10?crid=O539PSRXQE6I&#038;keywords=instant+coffee+for+camping&#038;qid=1642080928&#038;sprefix=instant+coffee+for+campi%2Caps%2C353&#038;sr=8-10"><span style="font-weight: 400;">instant coffee</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> with you on a camping trip, despite the bad reputation. The beans of brewed coffee are used to produce instant coffee granules, which are also known as a coffee powder or coffee crystals. Travelers who are backpacking and want to reduce their weight and space often use instant coffee because it’s lightweight.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-184 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-235 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-185 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-160">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated"><b>2. Use A Coffee Bag</b></h2>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Best for those who want it the ‘easy way’! </span></p>




<p><a href="https://www.amazon.com/100Pcs-Coffee-Filter-Paper-Bag/dp/B07XTHJK2S/ref=sr_1_1?crid=31WJ1FII5RAJV&#038;keywords=coffee+bag+for+camping&#038;qid=1642080993&#038;sprefix=coffee+ba+for+camping%2Caps%2C270&#038;sr=8-1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The coffee bag</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is similar to a teabag in that it is a quick, convenient way to brew coffee when camping. Whether you buy them in stores or make them yourself, these bags are thrown in boiling water and steeped in order to make coffee.</span></p>




<p><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">It’s just that simple.</span></i></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Their small size, ease to clean up, and no expertise is required for them to brew make them ideal for traveling.</span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">These are the <a href="https://www.thatscoffee.com/category/best-sellers/">perfect coffees</a> for those who cannot handle anything more complicated (although because the beans aren’t freshly ground, it is slightly better than average).</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-186 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-238 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-161">

<p> <b style="color: var(--h2_typography-color); font-family: var(--h2_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h2_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h2_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3. The Java Drip Portable Coffee System</b><span style="color: var(--h2_typography-color); font-family: var(--h2_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h2_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h2_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">When it comes to camping, convenience is key, and the Java Drip fills all the boxes – it’s lightweight, BPA-free, and unbreakable, so you can bring it anywhere you go.</span></p>




<p><a href="https://www.amazon.com/GSI-Outdoors-JavaDrip-Coffee-50-Fluid-Ounce/dp/B00OHCLO98/ref=sr_1_5?crid=3KALDJSSYWQ2U&#038;keywords=java%2Bdrip%2Bfor%2Bbackpacking&#038;qid=1642081019&#038;sprefix=java%2Bdrip%2Caps%2C274&#038;sr=8-5&#038;th=1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The GSI JavaDrip ultralight coffee maker</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> was designed for backpacking enthusiasts who wanted to drink great coffee outdoors without sacrificing weight or space in their backpack.</span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This little half-ounce brewer is made of nylon and plastic, so it can keep your drinks hot for weeks.</span></p>

<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-188 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-239 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-162">

<h2 data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px" class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontSize:26; line-height: 1.1; --minFontSize:26;"><b>4. Cowboy Coffee Camping</b></h2>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The art of making cowboy coffee may be disappearing with today’s technology. Nevertheless, cowboy coffee is just as simple, if not more, than an instant for camping. To enjoy your next camping trip in true cowboy fashion, learn how to make this simple coffee!  </span></p>




<ol>


<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Start by establishing your heat source</span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Fill your camping coffee maker with COLD water</span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Stir in 1 heaping tablespoon of coarse ground coffee per 1 12 cups of water</span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Apply heat until the desired brewing temperature is achieved.</span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Remove from heat, add a shot of cold water, and allow the grounds to settle </span></li>




<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Pour and enjoy!</span></li>


</ol>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-189 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-240 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-47 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="coffee by the fire" title="coffee by the fire" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20626" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/alex-holt-UpGI7J2ek5s-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-190 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-241 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-163">

<h2><b>5. Use Single Serve Filters</b></h2>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Purchase a </span><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Tupkee-Coffee-Filters-4-6-Cups/dp/B081MWZQVK/ref=sr_1_3_sspa?crid=23OFDGUEHQOJF&#038;keywords=single+serve+coffee+filter&#038;qid=1642081059&#038;sprefix=single+serve+coffee+filt%2Caps%2C287&#038;sr=8-3-spons&#038;psc=1&#038;spLa=ZW5jcnlwdGVkUXVhbGlmaWVyPUExSkZXTzdOOU82WFdBJmVuY3J5cHRlZElkPUEwNjgyMDA3MUwwQ0ZDTVBGUjFDQSZlbmNyeXB0ZWRBZElkPUEwMTM5ODgwWllYVDdDR1JOSUZCJndpZGdldE5hbWU9c3BfYXRmJmFjdGlvbj1jbGlja1JlZGlyZWN0JmRvTm90TG9nQ2xpY2s9dHJ1ZQ=="><span style="font-weight: 400;">single-serve filter</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> to achieve the portability of the MacGyver method. </span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">One of the easiest filters to carry on this list is Presuma’s single-serve filter, since it lies flat when not in use. Others require a little more space. Whenever you’re backpacking, this is probably the best way to brew coffee. </span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Use a pour-over method with this filter. Put the coffee grounds in the filter first. When the water is boiling, let it cool for a few minutes until it is only slightly warm but not boiling. Once the water is warm, slowly pour it over the grounds. Allow the coffee to bloom for a bit before adding the remaining water. </span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Pour the remaining liquid and coffee oils into the filter and lift it above your cup for an extra burst of flavor. Enjoy right away. </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-191 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-242 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-48 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1827" alt="pouring into coffee filter" title="pouring into coffee filter" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20627" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-200x143-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-400x285-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-600x428-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-800x571-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-1200x856-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/tyler-nix-WVl1N2C2zEA-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-192 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-243 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-164">

<p><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Overall, here’s the answer to the million-dollar question: how do you make coffee while camping? Ready? </span></i></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The easiest way to enjoy decent coffee before hiking is to pack along a few instant coffee packs – and a way to heat the water.</span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You might also consider the collapsible pour-over filter we mentioned above if you like to adjust the brewing process. </span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The only thing you’ll miss while camping is your hot shower, but fortunately not your coffee. Whatever your travel circumstances may be, you can still prepare fresh, hot coffee every day, whether you’re backpacking in </span><a href="https://www.liftylife.ca/vancouver-to-whistler-top-sea-to-sky-stops/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Vancouver</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, sleeping on the side of a mountain, or glamping in an RV.</span></p>




<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">When you’re feeling adventurous, consider one of these easy methods to brew coffee while camping! </span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-244 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-8 fusion-title-text fusion-title-size-one">

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-left fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

<span class="awb-title-spacer fusion-no-large-visibility fusion-no-medium-visibility fusion-no-small-visibility"></span>

<h1 class="title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.1;"><b style="color: var(--h1_typography-color); font-family: var(--h1_typography-font-family); font-size: var(--h1_typography-font-size); font-style: var(--h1_typography-font-style,normal); letter-spacing: var(--h1_typography-letter-spacing); background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Eco-Friendly, Zero-Waste Airbnb Vacation Rental Furnishing</b></h1>

<span class="awb-title-spacer"></span>

<div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">

<div class="title-sep sep- sep-solid" style="border-color:#e0dede;"></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-245 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-165">

<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The only way to protect the Earth is to hold yourself accountable for your actions.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;">You can make simple and affordable improvements in your vacation rental to create a more sustainable hosting. Plus furnishing your Airbnb as eco-friendly can be a great point of differentiation and competitive advantages against competitors. Sometimes it pays to go green!</p>


</div>



<div class="fusion-image-element " style="--awb-caption-title-size:var(--h2_typography-font-size);--awb-caption-title-transform:var(--h2_typography-text-transform);--awb-caption-title-line-height:var(--h2_typography-line-height);--awb-caption-title-letter-spacing:var(--h2_typography-letter-spacing);"><span class=" fusion-imageframe imageframe-none imageframe-49 hover-type-none"><img decoding="async" width="2560" height="1707" alt="eco-friendly products" title="eco-friendly products" src="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg" class="img-responsive wp-image-20593" srcset="https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-200x133-1.jpg 200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-400x267-1.jpg 400w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-600x400-1.jpg 600w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-800x533-1.jpg 800w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-1200x800-1.jpg 1200w, https://blog.hichee.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/anna-oliinyk-nCPpMv69m1s-unsplash-scaled-1.jpg 2560w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, (max-width: 640px) 100vw, 800px" /></span></div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-194 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-246 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-166">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"></h2>




<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="--fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>How Can Eco-friendly Alternatives Help?</b></h2>




<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b style="color: #0f7375;">Changing the world for the better</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">It is relatively easy to reduce the amount of waste produced by your Airbnb by taking simple steps. Opt for <a style="font-weight: 400;" href="https://www.liftylife.ca/airbnb-host-checklist/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">eco-friendly alternatives</a> in your Airbnb furnishing and stocking. Reducing waste and omissions is a necessary goal for everyone in order to keep our planet healthy.</p>




<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b style="color: #0f7375;">A cost-effective solution</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;">If you avoid single-use toiletries and reusable towels, you can significantly lower your purchase costs. Being an Airbnb host not only helps the environment but also helps you to save money. Purchasing in bulk and using a refillery can be a cost saving strategy in the long term.</p>




<h3 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 24; line-height: 1.67; --minfontsize: 24;" data-fontsize="24" data-lineheight="40.08px"><b style="color: #0f7375;">A free marketing campaign for Airbnb</b></h3>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guests at Airbnb are frequently looking for ways to reduce their carbon footprint. You can therefore market your Airbnb as green and attract like-minded guests to stay at your house.</span></p>




<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here are a few eco-friendly, zero-waste Airbnb supplies and products for Airbnb guests that will reduce your carbon footprint.</span></p>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>



<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-195 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;" >

<div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start" style="max-width:1216.8px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );">

<div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-247 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:1.92%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:20px;--awb-spacing-left-large:1.92%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;">

<div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column">

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-167">

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>Eco-friendly Kitchen Supplies</b></h2>




<ul>

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-169">

<h2 style="text-align: justify;"><b> Eco-friendly Furnishing</b></h2>




<ul>


<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Offer reusable grocery bags for guests’ convenience</span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Buy durable, good-quality furnishings for your rental property. It will save you both money and landfill space.</span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consider using wood, bamboo, cotton, jute, or wool where possible (instead of plastic, vinyl, or PVC – synthetic materials)</span></li>


</ul>

<h2 class="fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="text-align: justify; --fontsize: 26; line-height: 1.1; --minfontsize: 26;" data-fontsize="26" data-lineheight="28.6px"><b>Other Eco-friendly Supplies for Airbnb </b></h2>




<ul>


<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Use <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0170RW9D6/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#038;camp=1789&#038;creative=9325&#038;creativeASIN=B0170RW9D6&#038;linkCode=as2&#038;tag=liftylife0c-20&#038;linkId=467b94180c806fe2f5e40a126d81cf62" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">cleaning products that are eco-friendly</a> or plant-based</span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Make your Airbnb rental more energy-efficient by installing <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B08J87MTXF/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#038;camp=1789&#038;creative=9325&#038;creativeASIN=B08J87MTXF&#038;linkCode=as2&#038;tag=liftylife0c-20&#038;linkId=082b52f0015a2fcc7c46c7fab721f9e2" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">LED lights</a>.</span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Decorate the Airbnb rental with plenty of <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B09K9GW3BH/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#038;camp=1789&#038;creative=9325&#038;creativeASIN=B09K9GW3BH&#038;linkCode=as2&#038;tag=liftylife0c-20&#038;linkId=d414a15a874fcaf8928ac6675f62642e" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">indoor plants</a>. </span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Provide your guests with thermostat and water temperature recommendations to prevent them from experimenting and potentially using more energy than necessary.</span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Maintain a household <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0087S48E6/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#038;camp=1789&#038;creative=9325&#038;creativeASIN=B0087S48E6&#038;linkCode=as2&#038;tag=liftylife0c-20&#038;linkId=dbbd00c3c6f33d15a4480100570bb4ac" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">recycling system </a></span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Place a donation box </span></li>




<li style="text-align: justify; font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Encourage guests to conserve water and electricity by pasting friendly notes around the rental </span></li>


</ul>


</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="fusion-text fusion-text-171">

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Little drops of water make the mighty ocean. So, as a host, you can take these little steps towards carbon-neutrality by promoting these eco-friendly, zero-waste Airbnb supplies and products! A vacation rental can be luxury, but true luxury is when your guests are soulfully pleased and so is the environment. </span></p>
